rule ("global init") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    actions {
        Disable Inspector Recording;
        Set Global Variable(subtitle_speed, Workshop Setting Real(Custom String("General"), Custom String("Subtitle speed"), 4, 1, 10, 1));
        Set Global Variable(difficulty, Subtract(Workshop Setting Combo(Custom String("General"), Custom String("Difficulty"), 3, Array(Custom String("Cinematic‚Ä®"), Custom String("Dead Easy‚Ä®"), Custom String("Para-Normal‚Ä®"), Custom String("Terrifying!‚Ä®"), Custom String("JUNKTASTICALLY NIGHTMARISH!!!")), 0), 1));
        Set Global Variable(newline, Custom String("\n"));
        Create HUD Text(All Players(All Teams), Null, Null, Custom String(" {0}{0}{1}{2}", Custom String("{0}{0}{0}{0}{0}{0}{0}{0}{0}", Global.newline), Global.newline, If-Then-Else(Or(Global.objective_complete, Global.no_hud), Custom String("{0}{0}{0}{0}", Global.newline), Custom String(" "))), Top, True, Null, Null, Color(White), Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Set Global Variable(t2_names_array, Array(Custom String("The Witch"), Custom String("Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein"), Custom String("Junkenstein's Monster"), Custom String("The Reaper"), Null, Custom String("The Swordsman"), Custom String("The Merchant"), Custom String("The Gunslinger"), Custom String("The Summoner"), Custom String("The Alchemist"), Null));
        Set Global Variable(t2_heroes_array, Array(Hero(Mercy), Hero(Junkrat), Hero(Roadhog), Hero(Reaper), Hero(Reinhardt), Hero(Genji), Hero(Moira), Hero(Cassidy), Hero(Symmetra), Hero(Ana), Hero(Sombra)));
        Set Global Variable(t2_hero_colours, Array(Custom Color(246, 231, 100, 255), Custom Color(False, 255, 255, 255), Custom Color(62, 219, 54, 255), Custom Color(173, False, False, 255), Color(White), Custom Color(100, 255, 100, 255), Custom Color(130, 40, 255, 255), Custom Color(255, 50, 50, 255), Custom Color(255, 119, False, 255), Custom Color(54, 114, 255, 255), Custom Color(169, 135, 255, 255)));
        Set Global Variable(name_colors_2, Array(Custom Color(255, 250, 204, 255), Custom Color(156, 255, 255, 255), Custom Color(162, 207, 159, 255), Custom Color(196, 84, 84, 255)));
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        For Global Variable(i5, 0, 3, True);
            Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Cloud, Color(White), Vector(73.565, 11.5, -78.868), 7, Visible To Position and Radius);
            Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Cloud, Color(White), Vector(71.114, 11.5, -85.222), 7, Visible To Position and Radius);
            Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Cloud, Color(White), Vector(91.835, 9, -88.522), 7, Visible To Position and Radius);
            Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Cloud, Color(White), Vector(96.558, 9, -83.995), 7, Visible To Position and Radius);
            Set Global Variable(spawn_corners, Array(Vector(False, False, -5.25), Vector(-24.09, False, -8.49)));
            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Set Global Variable(spawn_line, Vector Towards(First Of(Global.spawn_corners), Last Of(Global.spawn_corners)));
        Pause Match Time;
        Create HUD Text(Filtered Array(All Players(All Teams), Not(Or(Or(Global.objective_complete, Global.no_hud), (Current Array Element).shop))), Custom String(" {0}   OBJECTIVE: {1}   {0}", Global.newline, Global.objective), Null, Null, Top, False, Custom Color(Global.obj_color_r, Global.obj_color_g, Global.obj_color_b, 255), Null, Null, Visible To String and Color, Default Visibility);
        Set Global Variable(objective, Custom String("Wait for players to assemble."));
        Start Rule(obj_color, Restart Rule);
        Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring, Color(Aqua), Global.skip_cutscene_pos, 2, Visible To Position and Radius);
        Create In-World Text(If-Then-Else(Compare(Y Component Of(Global.skip_cutscene_pos), <, 900), All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Custom String("Group up here to skip the dialogue!"), Global.skip_cutscene_pos, 1.2, Do Not Clip, Visible To Position and String, Color(Aqua), Default Visibility);
        Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring, Color(Green), Global.objective_pos, 4, Visible To Position and Radius);
        Create Icon(Filtered Array(All Players(All Teams), And(Compare(Y Component Of(Global.objective_pos), <, 900), Not((Current Array Element).shop))), Global.objective_pos, Arrow: Down, Visible To and Position, Color(Green), True);
        Create HUD Text(All Players(All Teams), Null, Null, Custom String(" \n\n\n\n"), Left, False, Null, Null, Color(White), Visible To, Default Visibility);
        Set Global Variable(boundary_corners, Array(Vector(12.6, 6, -118.814), Vector(42.805, 6, -44.411)));
        Set Global Variable(boundary_line, Vector Towards(First Of(Global.boundary_corners), Last Of(Global.boundary_corners)));
        Create HUD Text(All Players(Team 2), Custom String("  Money:‚Ä®‚Ç¨{0}{1}  ", (Local Player).euros, If-Then-Else(Compare((Local Player).real, >, False), Custom String(" + R${0}", (Local Player).real), Custom String(""))), Custom String(" "), Custom String(" "), Right, -0.49, Custom Color(150, 255, 175, 255), Color(White), Color(White), Visible To String and Color, Default Visibility);
        Set Global Variable(shop_campos, Array(Vector(-23.327, 7.679, -91.651), Vector(-21.86, 7.679, -94.904)));
        Set Global Variable(shop_left, Normalize(Cross Product(Direction Towards(First Of(Global.shop_campos), Last Of(Global.shop_campos)), Down)));
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);

        Set Global Variable(compressBakeResult, Empty Array);
        For Global Variable(compressBakeNodeLoop, 0, Count Of(Global.compressedNodes), True);
            Set Global Variable(compressCurrentNodeArray, Empty Array);
            For Global Variable(compressBakeStringLoop, 0, Count Of(Value In Array(Global.compressedNodes, Global.compressBakeNodeLoop)), True);
                Set Global Variable(compressMapper, Empty Array);
                Set Global Variable At Index(compressMapper, Subtract(String Length(Value In Array(Value In Array(Global.compressedNodes, Global.compressBakeNodeLoop), Global.compressBakeStringLoop)), True), Null);
                Modify Global Variable(compressCurrentNodeArray, Append To Array, Mapped Array(Global.compressMapper, Index Of String Char(Global.compressBakeMatcher, String Slice(Value In Array(Value In Array(Global.compressedNodes, Global.compressBakeNodeLoop), Global.compressBakeStringLoop), Current Array Index, 1))));

            End;
            Set Global Variable At Index(compressBakeResult, Global.compressBakeNodeLoop, Global.compressCurrentNodeArray);
        End;
        Set Global Variable At Index(_extendedGlobalCollection, True, Index Of Array Value(Global._classIndexes, Null));
        Set Global Variable At Index(_classIndexes, Value In Array(Global._extendedGlobalCollection, True), 2);
        Set Global Variable At Index(_objectVariable_1, Value In Array(Global._extendedGlobalCollection, True), Global.map);
        Set Global Variable At Index(_objectVariable_0, Value In Array(Global._extendedGlobalCollection, True), Global.compressBakeResult);
        Set Global Variable(bake, Value In Array(Global._extendedGlobalCollection, True));
        Set Global Variable(pathmapReference, Value In Array(Global._objectVariable_1, Global.bake));
        Set Global Variable(all_nodes, Value In Array(Global._objectVariable_0, Value In Array(Global._objectVariable_1, Global.bake)));
        Set Global Variable(lol2, Value In Array(Global._objectVariable_0, Global.bake));
        Set Global Variable(lol3, Value In Array(Global._objectVariable_0, Global.pathmapReference));
        Set Global Variable(lol4, Value In Array(Global._objectVariable_2, Global.pathmapReference));
        Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
        Set Global Variable(_classIndexes, Empty Array);
        Set Global Variable(_extendedGlobalCollection, Vector(9999, 9999, False));
        Set Global Variable(_tempNodes, Null);
        Set Global Variable(_tempSegments, Null);
        Set Global Variable(_tempAttributes, Null);
        Set Global Variable(map, Null);
        Set Global Variable(compressBakeMatcher, Vector(9999, -9999, False));
        Set Global Variable(compressedNodes, Null);
        Set Global Variable(compressBakeResult, Null);
        Set Global Variable(compressCurrentNodeArray, Null);
        Set Global Variable(compressBakeNodeLoop, Null);
        Set Global Variable(compressBakeStringLoop, Null);
        Set Global Variable(compressMapper, Null);
        Set Global Variable(_objectVariable_0, Null);
        Set Global Variable(_objectVariable_1, Null);
        Set Global Variable(_objectVariable_2, Null);
        Set Global Variable(objective_pos, Global._extendedGlobalCollection);
        Set Global Variable(skip_cutscene_pos, Global._extendedGlobalCollection);
    }
}

rule ("Pathfinder: Resolve Next") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
        (Event Player).start_pathfind == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, destination, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).zomnic, ==, 1), (Event Player).zomnic_dest, If-Then-Else((Event Player).piss_ending, Vector(111, 11.15, -5.36), Position Of((Event Player).target))));
        Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, Direction Towards(Position Of(Event Player), If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).pathfinderCurrent, ==, -1), (Event Player).destination, Value In Array(Global.lol3, (Event Player).pathfinderCurrent))), 1, To World, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, parentArray, Value In Array(Global.lol2, Index Of Array Value(Global.all_nodes, First Of(Sorted Array(Global.all_nodes, Add(Add(Distance Between(Current Array Element, (Event Player).destination), Multiply(1000, Compare(Vertical Angle From Direction(Direction Towards(Current Array Element, (Event Player).destination)), <, -50))), Multiply(1000, Not(Is In Line of Sight(Current Array Element, Add((Event Player).destination, Up), Barriers Do Not Block LOS)))))))));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, pathfinderCurrent, Index Of Array Value(Global.lol3, First Of(Sorted Array(Global.lol3, Add(Add(Add(Distance Between(Position Of(Event Player), Current Array Element), Distance Between(Position Of((Event Player).target), Current Array Element)), Multiply(1000, Compare(Vertical Angle From Direction(Direction Towards(Position Of(Event Player), Current Array Element)), <, -50))), Multiply(1000, Not(Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Add(Current Array Element, Up), Barriers Do Not Block LOS))))))));
        While(And(Is Alive(Event Player), (Event Player).start_pathfind));
            If(Compare(Distance Between(Position Of(Event Player), Value In Array(Global.lol3, (Event Player).pathfinderCurrent)), <=, 0.4));
                Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
                If(Not((Event Player).zomnic));
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, destination, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).zomnic, ==, 1), (Event Player).zomnic_dest, If-Then-Else((Event Player).piss_ending, Vector(111, 11.15, -5.36), Position Of((Event Player).target))));
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, parentArray, Value In Array(Global.lol2, Index Of Array Value(Global.all_nodes, First Of(Sorted Array(Global.all_nodes, Add(Add(Distance Between(Current Array Element, (Event Player).destination), Multiply(1000, Compare(Vertical Angle From Direction(Direction Towards(Current Array Element, (Event Player).destination)), <, -50))), Multiply(1000, Not(Is In Line of Sight(Current Array Element, Add((Event Player).destination, Up), Barriers Do Not Block LOS)))))))));
                End;
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, pathfinderCurrent, Subtract(Value In Array((Event Player).parentArray, (Event Player).pathfinderCurrent), True));
            End;
            Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        End;
    }
}

rule ("bot target") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
        (Event Player).ana_target_friends == False;
        Global.roar == False;
        (Event Player).hex == False;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, target, First Of(Sorted Array(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), And(Or(Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element)), And(And((Current Array Element).zomnic, Not((Event Player).boss_ID)), Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, !=, 10))), Not((Current Array Element).is_downed))), Add(Add(Distance Between(Event Player, Current Array Element), Multiply(1000, Not(Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position(Current Array Element), Barriers Do Not Block LOS)))), Multiply(1000, Compare(Vertical Angle From Direction(Direction Towards(Event Player, Current Array Element)), <, -50))))));
        Wait(5, Abort When False);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("bot pathfind too high/out of los") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
        (Event Player).pre_init == False;
        (Event Player).avoid_enviro == False;
    }
    actions {
        If(Not((Event Player).start_pathfind));
            If(Or(Not(Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Event Player).target), Barriers Do Not Block LOS)), Compare(Vertical Angle From Direction(Direction Towards(Event Player, (Event Player).target)), <, -50)));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, start_pathfind, True);
            End;
        End;
        If((Event Player).start_pathfind);
            If(Compare(Vertical Angle From Direction(Direction Towards(Event Player, (Event Player).target)), >, -30));
                If(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), <, 25));
                    If(Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Event Player).target), Barriers Do Not Block LOS));
                        Set Player Variable(Event Player, start_pathfind, False);
                    End;
                End;
            End;
        End;
        Wait(2, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, start_pathfind, False);
    }
}

rule ("narrator vocalisation") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Is Dummy Bot(Event Player) == False;
        Global.vocalisation == True;
        Array Contains(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Hero(Sombra)), Global.main_speaker) == True;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare(Global.main_speaker, ==, Hero(Reinhardt)));
            While(Global.vocalisation);
                Play Effect(Event Player, DVa Micro Missiles Explosion Sound, Color(White), If-Then-Else(Global.defeat, World Vector Of(Vector(False, True, 2), Global.last_player_to_die, Rotation And Translation), Add(Eye Position(Event Player), Facing Direction Of(Event Player))), If-Then-Else(Global.defeat, 200, 75));
                Wait(If-Then-Else(Global.defeat, 0.05, 0.1), Ignore Condition);
            End;
        Else;
            Create Effect(Event Player, Sombra Hacking Sound, Team 1, Add(Eye Position(Event Player), Facing Direction Of(Event Player)), 200, Visible To Position and Radius);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, sombra_sound, Last Created Entity);
            Wait Until(Not(Global.vocalisation), 99999);
            Destroy Effect((Event Player).sombra_sound);
    }
}

rule ("main dialogue subr") {
    event {
        Subroutine;
        main_dialogue;
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(line_number, Null);
        For Global Variable(i_vocal, 0, Count Of(Global.active_dialogue_list), True);
            Set Global Variable(main_speaker, First Of(Value In Array(Global.active_dialogue_list, Global.line_number)));
            If(Not(Compare(Global.phase, ==, 20)));
                Start Forcing Player To Be Hero(Global.dialogue_bot, If-Then-Else(Global.ana_spawn_fix, Hero(Ana), Global.main_speaker));
            End;
            Set Global Variable(vocalisation, True);
            Set Global Variable(main_dialogue, Value In Array(Value In Array(Global.active_dialogue_list, Global.line_number), True));
            Set Global Variable(letter_scroll, Null);
            For Global Variable(i2_vocal, 0, String Length(Global.main_dialogue), True);
                Wait Until(Global.is_dialoguing, If-Then-Else(Global.defeat, 0.018, 0.035));
                Modify Global Variable(letter_scroll, Add, 1);
                If(Array Contains(Array(Custom String(", "), Custom String(". "), Custom String("? "), Custom String("! "), Custom String("- ")), String Slice(Global.main_dialogue, Subtract(Global.letter_scroll, True), 2)));
                    Set Global Variable(vocalisation, False);
                    Wait Until(Global.is_dialoguing, Multiply(If-Then-Else(Array Contains(Array(Custom String(","), Custom String("-")), Char In String(Global.main_dialogue, Subtract(Global.letter_scroll, True))), 0.25, 0.5), If-Then-Else(Global.defeat, 0.5, 1)));
                    Set Global Variable(vocalisation, True);
                End;
                If(Not(Modulo(Global.letter_scroll, 3)));
                    If(Compare(Global.main_speaker, !=, Hero(Reinhardt)));
                        If(And(Compare(Global.phase, ==, 20), Compare(Global.main_speaker, ==, Hero(Junkrat))));
                            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Junkrat Frag Launcher Explosion Sound, Team 2, Eye Position(Global.junkrat), 75);
                        Else If(Compare(Number Of Heroes(Global.main_speaker, All Teams), >, True));
                            Set Status(Global.dialogue_bot, Null, Hacked, 0.001);
                        End;
                    End;
                End;
                If(Global.is_dialoguing);
                    Break;
                End;
            End;
            Set Global Variable(vocalisation, False);
            Wait Until(Global.is_dialoguing, Multiply(Multiply(Value In Array(Value In Array(Global.active_dialogue_list, Global.line_number), 2), 0.5), Global.subtitle_speed));
            If(Global.is_dialoguing);
                Break;
            End;
            Modify Global Variable(line_number, Add, 1);
        End;
        Set Global Variable(main_dialogue, Null);
    }
}

rule ("has status") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Or(Or(Or(Has Status(Event Player, Stunned), Has Status(Event Player, Knocked Down)), Has Status(Event Player, Asleep)), And(Has Status(Event Player, Frozen), Compare(Not((Event Player).boss_ID), ==, 1))) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, has_status, True);
        While(Or(Or(Or(Has Status(Event Player, Stunned), Has Status(Event Player, Knocked Down)), Has Status(Event Player, Asleep)), Has Status(Event Player, Frozen)));
            Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, has_status, False);
    }
}

    event {
        Player Received Healing;
        All;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Event Was Health Pack == True;
    }
    actions {
        Clear Status(Event Player, Burning);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, poisoned, False);
    }
}

rule ("phased out/immort clear status") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Or(Has Status(Event Player, Phased Out), Has Status(Event Player, Invincible)) == True;
        Or(Has Status(Event Player, Burning), (Event Player).poisoned) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Abort If(Is Dummy Bot(Event Player));
        Clear Status(Event Player, Burning);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, poisoned, False);
    }
}

rule ("took knockback") {
    event {
        Player Received Knockback;
        All;
        All;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, took_knockback, 1);
        Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, took_knockback, False, True, None);
    }
}

rule ("pond") {
    event {
        Subroutine;
        pond;
    }
    actions {
        Apply Impulse(Event Player, Up, If-Then-Else(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Zenyatta)), 7, 0.001), To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
        If(And(And(Compare(Throttle Of(Event Player), ==, Vector(False, False, False)), Compare(Speed Of(Event Player), >, 0.5)), Not((Event Player).took_knockback)));
            Apply Impulse(Event Player, Forward, 0.001, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
            Apply Impulse(Event Player, Backward, 0.001, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
            Apply Impulse(Event Player, Left, 0.001, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
            Apply Impulse(Event Player, Right, 0.001, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
        Else If(And(Compare(Throttle Of(Event Player), !=, Vector(False, False, False)), Not((Event Player).took_knockback)));
            Apply Impulse(Event Player, Cross Product(World Vector Of(Throttle Of(Event Player), Event Player, Rotation), Up), 0.001, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
            Apply Impulse(Event Player, Cross Product(World Vector Of(Throttle Of(Event Player), Event Player, Rotation), Down), 0.001, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
            Apply Impulse(Event Player, World Vector Of(Throttle Of(Event Player), Event Player, Rotation), 0.001, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
        End;
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        If(Or(Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Jump)), (Event Player).bot_jump));
            Apply Impulse(Event Player, Up, 6, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
        End;
        Loop If Condition Is True;
        If(Compare((Event Player).zomnic, ==, 1));
            Call Subroutine(pathfind_init);
        End;
    }
}

    event {

    conditions {

        Y Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)) > 10;
        Z Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)) > -94;
        Z Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)) < -74;
    }
    actions {
        Call Subroutine(pond);
    }
}

rule ("bot stuck") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Is Dummy Bot(Event Player) == True;
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
        Throttle Of(Event Player) != Vector(False, False, False);
        Speed Of In Direction(Event Player, World Vector Of(Throttle Of(Event Player), Event Player, Rotation)) < 3;
    }
    actions {
        Abort If((Event Player).no_jump);
        Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
        Press Button(Event Player, Button(Jump));
        Apply Impulse(Event Player, Up, 7, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, bot_jump, True);
        Wait(1.5, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, bot_jump, False);
    }
}

rule ("bot stuck too long") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Is Dummy Bot(Event Player) == True;
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
        Throttle Of(Event Player) != Vector(False, False, False);
        Speed Of In Direction(Event Player, World Vector Of(Throttle Of(Event Player), Event Player, Rotation)) < 3;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(1.5, Abort When False);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, start_pathfind, False);
        Wait(Multiply(Global.wait, 3), Ignore Condition);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, start_pathfind, True);
    }
}

rule ("spawn doors") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(spawn_doors, Array(Vector(-12.054, 2.313, -6.509), Vector(-25.135, 2.279, -0.134), Vector(-0.763, 7.237, 0.767)));
        For Global Variable(i_vocal, 0, Count Of(Global.spawn_doors), True);
            Create In-World Text(Filtered Array(All Players(All Teams), Or(Not(Global.phase), (Current Array Element).egg)), Custom String("√ò"), Add(Value In Array(Global.spawn_doors, Evaluate Once(Global.i_vocal)), Vector(0, -0.7, 0)), 4, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To, Color(Red), Default Visibility);
            Modify Global Variable(spawn_door_effects, Append To Array, Last Text ID);
        End;
    }
}

rule ("player downed") {
    event {
        Player Died;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).is_downed == False;
        Is Dead(Event Player) == True;
        Is Dummy Bot(Event Player) == False;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare(Global.phase, >, 13));
            If(Compare(Global.phase, <, 23));
                If(Compare(Y Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)), <, 8));
                    Teleport(Event Player, Vector(77.842, 13.935, -98.146));
                    Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                End;
            End;
        End;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, killer, Attacker);
        If(Compare(Subtract(Value In Array((Event Player).potions, 8), (Event Player).extra_lives_used), >, False));
            If(Event Was Environment);
                Teleport(Event Player, Add(Nearest Walkable Position(Event Player), Multiply(Direction From Angles(Horizontal Angle From Direction(Direction Towards(Event Player, Nearest Walkable Position(Event Player))), -10), 2)));
                Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
            End;
            Resurrect(Event Player);
            Set Status(Event Player, Null, Phased Out, True);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Pharah Concussive Blast Effect, Team 2, Eye Position(Event Player), 1);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Moira Fade Disappear Sound, Team 1, Eye Position(Event Player), 200);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Sombra Translocating Material Effect, Team 2, Event Player, 1);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Sigma Accretion Impact Sound, Team 1, Eye Position(Event Player), 200);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion, Color(Violet), Eye Position(Event Player), 30);
            If(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Roadhog)));
                If(Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 1));
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, nano, 10);
                End;
            End;
            Modify Player Variable(Event Player, extra_lives_used, Add, 1);
            Set Global Variable(_tempAttributes, Event Player);
        Else;
            If(Compare(Count Of(Filtered Array(All Living Players(Team 2), Not(Or(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element), (Current Array Element).is_downed)))), >, False));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, pos_cache, Add(Nearest Walkable Position(Event Player), Multiply(Direction From Angles(Horizontal Angle From Direction(Direction Towards(Event Player, Nearest Walkable Position(Event Player))), -10), 2)));
                If(Event Was Environment);
                    Resurrect(Event Player);
                    Teleport(Event Player, (Event Player).pos_cache);
                    Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
                    Kill(Event Player, Null);
                End;
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, is_downed, True);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, death_timer, 40);
                Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, death_timer, False, True, Destination and Rate);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, revive_timer, 8);
                Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, revive_timer);
                Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 200);
                Set Global Variable(_tempNodes, Event Player);
            Else;
                Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 200);
                Set Global Variable(last_player_to_die, Event Player);
    }
}

rule ("player reviving") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).is_downed == True;
    }
    actions {
        Wait Until(Compare((Event Player).rezzing_players, !=, Empty Array), 99999);
        Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, revive_timer, False, Multiply(Add(0.666, Multiply(0.333, Count Of((Event Player).rezzing_players))), If-Then-Else(And(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Roadhog)), Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 1)), 2, 1)), Destination and Rate);
        Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
        Wait Until(Or(Compare((Event Player).rezzing_players, ==, Empty Array), Compare((Event Player).revive_timer, ==, 8)), 99999);
        Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, revive_timer, 8, True, Destination and Rate);
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("player reviving 2") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).is_downed == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, rezzing_players, Filtered Array(All Living Players(Team 2), And(And(Not(Or(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element), (Current Array Element).is_downed)), Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position(Current Array Element), Barriers Do Not Block LOS)), Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, Current Array Element), <, 5))));
        Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("player pause death timer") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).zomnic == False;
        (Event Player).revive_timer < 8;
    }
    actions {
        Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, death_timer);
        Wait Until(Or(Compare((Event Player).revive_timer, ==, 8), Not((Event Player).is_downed)), 100);
        Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, death_timer, False, True, Destination and Rate);
    }
}

    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).is_downed == True;
        (Event Player).revive_timer == False;

    }

rule ("player alive again") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).is_downed == True;
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(0.1, Abort When False);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, is_downed, False);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Debuff Impact Sound, Team 2, Event Player, 200);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Pickup Effect, Color(Yellow), Event Player, 1);
        Set Status(Event Player, Null, Phased Out, True);
        Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, death_timer);
        Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, revive_timer);
        If(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, -1));
            Set Status(Event Player, Null, Unkillable, 99999);
        End;
        If(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Roadhog)));
            If(Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 1));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, nano, 10);
            End;
        End;
        Set Global Variable(_tempSegments, Event Player);
    }
}

rule ("downed dialogue") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global._tempNodes != Null;
    }
    actions {
        Abort If(Not(Array Contains(All Players(Team 2), Global._tempNodes)));
        Abort If(Compare(Global.dialogue_priority, >, False));
        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, True);
        Wait Until(Not(Global.main_dialogue), 99999);
        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, False);
        If(And(Compare(Global.phase, ==, 5), Compare(((Global._tempNodes).killer).boss_ID, >, False)));
            If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Mercy)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The Swordsman dispatched the Witch, and in doing so, his mind became clearer."), 1.5)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Junkrat)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The Swordsman cut Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein to the ground, silencing him for the moment."), 1.5)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Roadhog)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The Swordsman dispatched the hulking behemoth with ease, his attention turning to the next target."), 1.5)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Reaper)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The Swordsman banished the Reaper, who disappeared into the night."), 1.5)));
            End;
        Else If(And(Compare(Global.phase, ==, 14), Compare(((Global._tempNodes).killer).boss_ID, >, False)));
            If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Mercy)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The Gunslinger felt no joy in killing a woman, even one as twisted as the Witch of the Wilds."), 1.5)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Junkrat)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("With a well-aimed shot, the Gunslinger felled Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein. But the battle still raged‚Ä¶"), 1.5)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Roadhog)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("With a shot from his revolver, the Gunslinger dropped the monster, who fell to the ground with an earth-shaking thud."), 1.5)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Reaper)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The Gunslinger's shot found its mark, and the Reaper was destroyed."), 1.5)));
            End;
        Else If(And(Compare(Global.phase, ==, 20), Compare(((Global._tempNodes).killer).boss_ID, >, False)));
            If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Mercy)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The Alchemist proved stronger than the Witch, a victory to which she derived no small bit of satisfaction."), 1.5)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Junkrat)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The Alchemist killed Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein, breathing a sigh of relief."), 1.5)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Roadhog)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The Alchemist's concoctions coursed through the monster, and its body was destroyed from within."), 1.5)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Reaper)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The Alchemist slew the Reaper, feeling a moment of sadness for the man she had once known."), 1.5)));
            End;
        Else If(And(Compare(Global.phase, ==, 26), Compare(((Global._tempNodes).killer).boss_ID, >, False)));
            If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Mercy)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The Witch's magic was no match for the Lord's hammer, and she was struck down."), 1.5)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Junkrat)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("With a mighty swing, the Lord bested his adversary, the Mad Doctor, denying him his revenge‚Ä¶ for now."), 1.5)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Roadhog)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("Large as the monster was, the Lord's conviction was larger, and the frightening creature was bested."), 1.5)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Reaper)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The Lord made quick work of the Reaper, driving the cursed apparition back into the shadows."), 1.5)));
            End;
        Else;
            If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Mercy)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Random Value In Array(Array(Custom String("The Witch was thusly defeated. But her magic was known to defy death itself."), Custom String("The magical essence in the air faded away, as the Witch crumpled to the ground, motionless."), Custom String("The Witch's power over life and death was not enough, and she suc***bed to her wounds."))), 2)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Junkrat)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Random Value In Array(Array(Custom String("The mad Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein had been slain. But the Witch of the Wilds was not done with him. Not in the least."), Custom String("With one last laugh, Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein was silenced. But such evil has a way of returning to the world."), Custom String("Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein fell, but the Lord knew that the danger had not passed."))), 2)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Roadhog)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Random Value In Array(Array(Custom String("With a thunderous crash, the monster fell to the ground, all semblance of life, extinguished."), Custom String("Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein's creation had been slain, its eyes as lifeless as pale stone."), Custom String("The spark of life within the monster was gone, and its fearsome body became inanimate once more."))), 2)));
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempNodes), ==, Hero(Reaper)));
                Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Random Value In Array(Array(Custom String("The Reaper's body faded into the darkness of the night."), Custom String("The Reaper had been felled. But the Lord felt sure that he'd return."), Custom String("Accursed smoke dissipated into harmless mist as the Reaper was dispatched."))), 2)));
            End;
        End;
        Start Rule(main_dialogue, Restart Rule);
        Set Global Variable(_tempNodes, Null);
    }
}

rule ("revive dialogue") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global._tempSegments != Null;
    }
    actions {
        Abort If(Not(Array Contains(All Players(Team 2), Global._tempSegments)));
        Abort If(Compare(Global.dialogue_priority, >, False));
        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, True);
        Wait Until(Not(Global.main_dialogue), 99999);
        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, False);
        If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempSegments), ==, Hero(Mercy)));
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Random Value In Array(Array(Custom String("The Witch emerged from the night, brought back to the battle by some darker power."), Custom String("The Witch was not to be undone, and she emerged from the shadows once again."), Custom String("Not even her own death could overcome the potent magic of the Witch of the Wilds!"))), 2)));
        Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempSegments), ==, Hero(Junkrat)));
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Random Value In Array(Array(Custom String("What was that sound on the wind? The Doctor had returned!"), Custom String("Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein emerged again, for his night of terror was yet to reach its conclusion."), Custom String("Alas, Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein could not yet rest without his vengeance fulfilled!"))), 2)));
        Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempSegments), ==, Hero(Roadhog)));
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Random Value In Array(Array(Custom String("The ground shook and shuddered once again; the monster had returned."), Custom String("Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein was not yet finished - his monster rose again!"), Custom String("A looming shadow reappeared - Junkenstein's monster was alive once more!"))), 2)));
        Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global._tempSegments), ==, Hero(Reaper)));
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Random Value In Array(Array(Custom String("To the heroes' dismay, the Reaper was not so easily defeated."), Custom String("The shadows took shape, and coalesced back into the form of the Reaper."), Custom String("Out of the night, the Reaper returned."))), 2)));

        Set Global Variable(_tempSegments, Null);
    }
}

rule ("final death dialogue") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.last_player_to_die != Null;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(All Players(Team 2), is_downed, False);
        Set Global Variable(no_hud, True);
        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, True);
        Wait Until(Not(Global.main_dialogue), 99999);
        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, False);
        Set Global Variable(defeat, True);
        Start Facing(Global.last_player_to_die, Facing Direction Of(Global.last_player_to_die), False, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
        Start Camera(All Players(Team 2), Ray Cast Hit Position(Eye Position(Global.last_player_to_die), Evaluate Once(World Vector Of(Vector(False, 2, 4), Global.last_player_to_die, Rotation And Translation)), Null, Global.last_player_to_die, True), Position Of(Global.last_player_to_die), 30);
        Set Slow Motion(20);
        Set Global Variable(dialogue_priority, 3);
        Wait(0.7, Ignore Condition);
        If(Compare(Hero Of(Global.last_player_to_die), ==, Hero(Mercy)));
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("And as the Witch fell, her magic had no more power."), 0.3), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("Her loyal servants remained lifeless on the ground. And as morning dawned, the castle was safe."), 0.6)));
        Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global.last_player_to_die), ==, Hero(Junkrat)));
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("With one last laugh, Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein's body collapsed onto the flagstones,"), 0.3), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("and as the last of his laughter echoed from the walls of the castle, the battle was over, and the castle had been saved."), 0.6)));
        Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global.last_player_to_die), ==, Hero(Roadhog)));
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("And the monster fell, just as its creator."), 0.3), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("Exhausted, battered, bruised, the denizens of Adlersbrunn celebrated their victory, for tonight they were safe."), 0.6)));
        Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global.last_player_to_die), ==, Hero(Reaper)));
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The Reaper fell. The enchanted pumpkin where his head ought to have been, smashed against the flagstones."), 0.3), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The night was quiet, and the castle was safe."), 0.6)));
        Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Global.last_player_to_die), ==, Hero(Symmetra)));
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("A chill spread through the air as the Summoner's body turned to ash."), 0.3), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The first signs of the dawn crept over the horizon, and the castle was safe."), 0.6)));
        Else If(And(Compare(Hero Of(Global.last_player_to_die), ==, Hero(Reinhardt)), Compare(Global.last_player_to_die, ==, Global.boss)));
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("But alas, this story was not one of triumph. This was a story of tragedy."), 0.3), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("As the once-mighty Lord of Adlersbrunn toppled over, exhaling his last breath on this mortal coil,"), 0.3), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.sombra_egg, ==, 69), Custom String("A single tear rolled down his cheek, for he knew that Brazil was inevitable."), Custom String("A single tear rolled down his cheek, for he knew that Adlersbrunn was doomed.")), 0.3), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.sombra_egg, ==, 69), Custom String("Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein had his revenge, and the vuvuzelas sounded throughout the night."), Custom String("Tonight, Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein had his revenge, and the indomitable villains celebrated.")), 0.3), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.sombra_egg, ==, 69), Custom String("Ol√©. Ol√©. Ol√©. Eu sou brasileiro."), Custom String("This was their terrible, bitter victory.")), 0.6)));
        End;
        Set Slow Motion(40);
        Start Rule(main_dialogue, Restart Rule);
        Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
        Wait Until(Not(Global.main_dialogue), 99999);
        If(And(Compare(Hero Of(Global.last_player_to_die), ==, Hero(Reinhardt)), Compare(Global.last_player_to_die, ==, Global.boss)));
            Set Slow Motion(100);
            Stop Camera(All Players(Team 2));
            Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
            Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, True);
            Wait Until(Not(Global.main_dialogue), 99999);
            Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, False);
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Sombra), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.sombra_egg, ==, 69), Custom String("Parab√©ns. You've unlocked the brazil ending. Obrigado por jogar."), Custom String("Congratulations. You've unlocked the {0} ending. Thank you for playing.", Value In Array(String Split(Custom String("Cinematic/Dead Easy/Para-Normal/Terrifying/JUNKTASTICALLY NIGHTMARISH"), Custom String("/")), Add(Global.difficulty, 1)))), 1), Array(Hero(Sombra), Custom String("You can check out the creator's YouTube and Discord at ''bit.ly/therister''."), 1.5), Array(Hero(Sombra), Custom String("Try replaying this gamemode to test out the other scrolls, or tackle other difficulties."), 1), Array(Hero(Sombra), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.sombra_egg, ==, 69), Custom String("rsrsrsrsrsrsrs kkkkkkkkkkkkkkk kspoakpskopaksopaksopka"), Custom String("Who knows, perhaps you might even discover some secrets...")), 1.5)));
            Call Subroutine(main_dialogue);
            Declare Team Victory(Team 2);
        Else;
            Declare Team Victory(Team 1);
    }
}

rule ("player death timer end") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).is_downed == True;
        (Event Player).death_timer == False;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, is_downed, False);
        Set Global Variable(last_player_to_die, Event Player);
    }
}

rule ("no hud") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.no_hud == True;
    }
    actions {
        Disable Hero HUD(Event Player);
        Wait Until(Not(Global.no_hud), 99999);
        Enable Hero HUD(Event Player);
    }
}

rule ("burn status") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Has Status(Event Player, Burning) == True;
        (Event Player).burner != Empty Array;
    }
    actions {
        Damage(Event Player, If-Then-Else(Compare(Team Of(Event Player), ==, Team 1), (Event Player).burner, Null), If-Then-Else(Compare(Team Of(Event Player), ==, Team 1), 4, Add(1, Global.difficulty)));
        Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, burner, Empty Array);
    }
}

rule ("teammate bot say hi") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Is Dummy Bot(Event Player) == False;
        Is Communicating(Event Player, Hello) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(0.5, Ignore Condition);
        Communicate(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element)), Hello);
    }
}

rule ("late joiner") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).late_join_check == False;
        Global.phase > 0.5;
        Is Dummy Bot(Event Player) == False;
        Has Spawned(Event Player) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Teleport(Event Player, Random Value In Array(Filtered Array(Remove From Array(All Players(Team 2), Event Player), Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element)))));
        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If(Is In Spawn Room(Event Player));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, late_join_check, True);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, euros, Global.euros_total);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, real, Global.real_total);
        Stop Camera(Event Player);
    }
}

rule ("player dealt damage") {
    event {
        Player Dealt Damage;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    actions {
        If(Value In Array((Event Player).potions, 6));
            Heal(Event Player, Null, Multiply(Multiply(Event Damage, Value In Array((Event Player).potions, 6)), 0.05));
        End;
        If(Value In Array((Event Player).potions, 7));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, random, Random Real(0, 20));
            If(And(Compare((Event Player).random, <, Value In Array((Event Player).potions, 7)), Compare(Event Ability, !=, Null)));
                Modify Player Variable(Victim, burner, Append To Array, Event Player);
                Set Status(Victim, Event Player, Burning, 3);
    }
}

rule ("destroy bound effects subr") {
    event {
        Subroutine;
        delete_bound_effects;
    }
    actions {
        While(Compare(Global.boundary_effects, !=, Empty Array));
            Destroy Effect(First Of(Global.boundary_effects));
            Modify Global Variable(boundary_effects, Remove From Array By Index, False);
            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        If(Compare(Global.phase, <, 10));
            For Global Variable(i5, 0, 3, True);
                Create Beam Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Beam, Add(First Of(Global.boundary_corners), Multiply(Vector(0, 1.5, 0), Evaluate Once(Global.i5))), Add(Last Of(Global.boundary_corners), Multiply(Vector(0, 1.5, 0), Evaluate Once(Global.i5))), Color(Gray), Visible To);
                Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
            End;
            Create Beam Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Beam, Vector(90.319, 20.596, -62.974), Vector(88.386, 23.292, -62.407), Color(Gray), Visible To);
            Create Beam Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Beam, Vector(90.337, 23.292, -62.964), Vector(88.386, 20.596, -62.407), Color(Gray), Visible To);
        End;
    }
}

rule ("enter shop") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.shop_open == True;
        (Event Player).shop == False;
        Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Interact)) == True;
        Distance Between(Event Player, Global.merchant) <= 3;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop, 1);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, False);
        Create In-World Text(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("Shopping..."), Event Player, True, Do Not Clip, Visible To Position and String, Color(Purple), Default Visibility);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, is_shopping_text_ID, Last Text ID);
        Start Camera(Event Player, First Of(Global.shop_campos), Last Of(Global.shop_campos), 0);
        Disable Hero HUD(Event Player);
        Set Move Speed(Event Player, 0.001);
        Disallow Button(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire));
        Disallow Button(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire));
        Disallow Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
        Disallow Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 2));
        Disallow Button(Event Player, Button(Ultimate));
        Disallow Button(Event Player, Button(Jump));
        Disallow Button(Event Player, Button(Crouch));
        Disallow Button(Event Player, Button(Melee));
        Disallow Button(Event Player, Button(Reload));
        If(Not((Event Player).max_health));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, max_health, Max Health(Event Player));
        End;
        Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, False);
    }
}

rule ("shop select") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).shop != False;
        Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire)) == True;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, 69));
            If(Compare((Event Player).shop, ==, 1));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop, False);
            Else;
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop, 1);
            End;
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, Null);
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).shop, ==, 1));
            If(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, Null));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop, 2);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, Null);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, 1));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop, 3);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, Null);
            End;
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).shop, ==, 2));
            If(Compare(Value In Array((Event Player).potions, (Event Player).shop_selection), >=, Value In Array((Event Player).potions_max, (Event Player).shop_selection)));
                Small Message(Event Player, Custom String("Out of stock!"));
                Play Effect(Event Player, Sombra Translocator Reappear Sound, Color(White), First Of(Global.shop_campos), 200);
            Else;
                If(Compare((Event Player).euros, <, Value In Array(Global.potions_price, (Event Player).shop_selection)));
                    Small Message(Event Player, Custom String("You cannot afford this item."));
                    Play Effect(Event Player, Sombra Translocator Reappear Sound, Color(White), First Of(Global.shop_campos), 200);
                Else;
                    Modify Player Variable At Index(Event Player, potions, (Event Player).shop_selection, Add, 1);
                    Play Effect(Event Player, Brigitte Repair Pack Impact Sound, Color(White), First Of(Global.shop_campos), 200);
                    Play Effect(Event Player, Good Pickup Effect, Color(Purple), (Global.merchant).attack, 1);
                    Modify Player Variable(Event Player, euros, Subtract, Value In Array(Global.potions_price, (Event Player).shop_selection));
                    Communicate((Global.merchant).attack, Thanks);
                End;
            End;
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).shop, ==, 3));
            If(Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, Value In Array((Event Player).scrolls_random, (Event Player).shop_selection)));
                Small Message(Event Player, Custom String("Already unlocked!"));
                Play Effect(Event Player, Sombra Translocator Reappear Sound, Color(White), First Of(Global.shop_campos), 200);
            Else;
                If(Compare((Event Player).real, <, 100));
                    Small Message(Event Player, Custom String("You cannot afford this scroll."));
                    Play Effect(Event Player, Sombra Translocator Reappear Sound, Color(White), First Of(Global.shop_campos), 200);
                Else;
                    Modify Player Variable(Event Player, scrolls_equip, Append To Array, Value In Array((Event Player).scrolls_random, (Event Player).shop_selection));
                    Play Effect(Event Player, Sombra Logo Sound, Color(White), First Of(Global.shop_campos), 200);
                    Play Effect(Event Player, Good Pickup Effect, Color(Yellow), (Global.merchant).attack, 1);
                    Modify Player Variable(Event Player, real, Subtract, 100);
                    Communicate((Global.merchant).attack, Thanks);
    }
}

rule ("shop 1 selection left right") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).shop == 1;
        Absolute Value(X Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player))) > 0.5;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare(X Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player)), >, False));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, If-Then-Else((Event Player).shop_selection, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, 69), 1, Null), 69));
        Else;
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, If-Then-Else((Event Player).shop_selection, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, 69), Null, 69), 1));
        End;
        Wait(0.2, Abort When False);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("shop 1 selection up down") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).shop == 1;
        Absolute Value(Z Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player))) > 0.5;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, 69), 1, 69));
        Wait(0.2, Abort When False);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("shop 2/3 selection left right") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Array Contains(Array(2, 3), (Event Player).shop) == True;
        Absolute Value(X Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player))) > 0.5;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare((Event Player).shop, ==, 2));
            If(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, 69));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, If-Then-Else(Compare(X Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player)), <, False), Null, 9));
            Else If(Or(And(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, 9), Compare(X Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player)), <, False)), And(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, Null), Compare(X Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player)), >, False))));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, 69);
            Else;
                If(Compare(X Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player)), >, False));
                    Modify Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, Add, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, <, 5), 4, -5));
                Else;
                    Modify Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, Add, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, <, 5), 5, -4));
                End;
            End;
        Else;
            If(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, 69));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, If-Then-Else(Compare(X Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player)), <, False), Null, 5));
            Else If(Or(And(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, 5), Compare(X Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player)), <, False)), And(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, Null), Compare(X Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player)), >, False))));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, 69);
            Else;
                If(Compare(X Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player)), >, False));
                    Modify Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, Add, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, <, 3), 2, -3));
                Else;
                    Modify Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, Add, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, <, 3), 3, -2));
                End;
            End;
        End;
        Wait(0.2, Abort When False);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("shop 2/3 selection up down") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Array Contains(Array(2, 3), (Event Player).shop) == True;
        Absolute Value(Z Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player))) > 0.5;
    }
    actions {
        Modify Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, Add, If-Then-Else(Compare(Z Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player)), >, False), -1, 1));
        If(Or(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).shop, ==, 2), 10, 6)), Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, -1)));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, 69);
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, 70));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, Null);
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).shop_selection, ==, 68));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).shop, ==, 2), 9, 5));
        End;
        Wait(0.2, Abort When False);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("shop go back") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).shop != False;
        Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire)) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).shop, ==, 1), Null, 1));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, shop_selection, Null);
    }
}

rule ("shop leave") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).shop == False;
    }
    actions {
        Stop Camera(Event Player);
        Enable Hero HUD(Event Player);
        Allow Button(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire));
        Allow Button(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire));
        Allow Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
        Allow Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 2));
        Allow Button(Event Player, Button(Ultimate));
        Allow Button(Event Player, Button(Jump));
        Allow Button(Event Player, Button(Crouch));
        Allow Button(Event Player, Button(Melee));
        Allow Button(Event Player, Button(Reload));
        Destroy In-World Text((Event Player).is_shopping_text_ID);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_dealt, Add(100, Multiply(First Of((Event Player).potions), 5)));
        Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_dealt);
        Set Healing Dealt(Event Player, Add(100, Multiply(Value In Array((Event Player).potions, True), 5)));
        Set Max Health(Event Player, Add(100, Divide(Multiply(2000, Value In Array((Event Player).potions, 2)), (Event Player).max_health)));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, speed, Add(100, Multiply(Value In Array((Event Player).potions, 3), 5)));
        Set Move Speed(Event Player, (Event Player).speed);
        If(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Mercy)));
            If(Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 2));
                Disallow Button(Event Player, (Event Player).button_damageboost);
            End;
            If(Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 4));
                Set Ability 2 Enabled(Event Player, False);
            End;
        End;
        If(Not((Event Player).max_ammo));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, max_ammo, Max Ammo(Event Player, False));
        End;
        Set Max Ammo(Event Player, False, Add((Event Player).max_ammo, Divide(Multiply(Value In Array((Event Player).potions, 4), (Event Player).max_ammo), 5)));
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Set Player Health(Event Player, 99999);
        Set Ammo(Event Player, False, Max Ammo(Event Player, False));
        If(Not(First Of((Event Player).create_scroll)));
            If(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Roadhog)));
                If(Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 2));
                    Create Effect(If-Then-Else(And(Is Crouching(Event Player), Compare(Health(Event Player), >, 100)), All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Mercy Damage Boosted Effect, Team 2, Event Player, True, Visible To Position and Radius);
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, create_scroll, True);
                End;
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Junkrat)));
                If(Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 1));
                    Create Effect(If-Then-Else(And(Compare(Normalized Health(Event Player), <, 0.666), Is Alive(Event Player)), All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Winston Tesla Cannon Target Effect, Team 2, Event Player, True, Visible To Position and Radius);
                    Create Effect(If-Then-Else(And(Compare(Normalized Health(Event Player), <, 0.666), Is Alive(Event Player)), All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Winston Tesla Cannon Target Sound, Team 2, Event Player, 200, Visible To Position and Radius);
                    Create Effect(If-Then-Else(And(Compare(Normalized Health(Event Player), <, 0.666), Is Alive(Event Player)), All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Ring, Color(White), Event Player, 8, Visible To Position and Radius);
                    Create Beam Effect(If-Then-Else(And(Compare(Normalized Health(Event Player), <, 0.666), Is Alive(Event Player)), All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Winston Tesla Cannon Beam, Event Player, Value In Array(If-Then-Else(Compare(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 8, Team 1, Surfaces), ==, Empty Array), Event Player, Append To Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 8, Team 1, Surfaces), Event Player)), Modulo(Multiply(Total Time Elapsed, 3), Count Of(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 8, Team 1, Surfaces)))), Team 2, Visible To Position and Radius);
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, create_scroll, True);
                End;
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Reaper)));
                If(Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 1));
                    Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Zenyatta Orb of Discord Target Effect, Team 2, (Event Player).death_mark, True, Visible To Position and Radius);
                    Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Zenyatta Orb of Discord Target Sound, Team 2, (Event Player).death_mark, 200, Visible To Position and Radius);
                    Create Icon(If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).death_mark, !=, Null), All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), (Event Player).death_mark, Skull, Visible To and Position, Color(Violet), False);
                    Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, create_scroll, False, True);
                End;
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Mercy)));
                If(Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 2));
                    Create Beam Effect(All Players(All Teams), Moira Grasp Connected Beam, If-Then-Else((Event Player).is_grasping, Add(Add(Add(Eye Position(Event Player), Facing Direction Of(Event Player)), Multiply(World Vector Of(Right, Event Player, Rotation), 0.1)), Multiply(Normalize(Cross Product(Facing Direction Of(Event Player), World Vector Of(Right, Event Player, Rotation))), 0.1)), Global._extendedGlobalCollection), If-Then-Else((Event Player).is_grasping, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).damage_target, !=, Null), (Event Player).damage_target, Add(Add(Add(Eye Position(Event Player), Facing Direction Of(Event Player)), Multiply(World Vector Of(Right, Event Player, Rotation), 0.1)), Multiply(Normalize(Cross Product(Facing Direction Of(Event Player), World Vector Of(Right, Event Player, Rotation))), 0.1))), Global._extendedGlobalCollection), Team 2, Visible To Position and Radius);
                    Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Mercy Damage Boosted Sound, Team 2, If-Then-Else((Event Player).is_grasping, Eye Position(Event Player), Global._extendedGlobalCollection), 200, Visible To Position and Radius);
                    Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, create_scroll, False, True);
                End;
            End;
        End;
        If(Not(Value In Array((Event Player).create_scroll, True)));
            If(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Reaper)));
                If(Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 3));
                    Create Effect(If-Then-Else(Is Using Ability 1(Event Player), All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Ring, Color(Violet), Event Player, 7, Visible To Position and Radius);
                    Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, create_scroll, True, True);
                End;
            Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Mercy)));
                If(Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, Null));
                    Start Healing Modification(Event Player, Event Player, 25, None);
                    Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, create_scroll, True, True);
                End;
            End;
        End;
        If(Not(Value In Array((Event Player).create_scroll, 2)));
            If(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Reaper)));
                If(Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 2));
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, scythe_swing, -1);
                    Create Beam Effect(If-Then-Else(Is Meleeing(Event Player), All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Grapple Beam, World Vector Of(Vector(0, 1.2, 0), Event Player, Rotation And Translation), Add(World Vector Of(Vector(0, 1.2, 0), Event Player, Rotation And Translation), Multiply(Add(Multiply(Sine From Degrees((Event Player).scythe_angle), Facing Direction Of(Event Player)), Multiply(Cosine From Degrees((Event Player).scythe_angle), World Vector Of(Vector(-1, Multiply(0.3, (Event Player).scythe_swing), False), Event Player, Rotation))), (Event Player).scythe_length)), Team 1, Visible To Position and Radius);
                    Create Beam Effect(If-Then-Else(Is Meleeing(Event Player), All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Omnic Slicer Beam, Add(World Vector Of(Vector(0, 1.2, 0), Event Player, Rotation And Translation), Multiply(Add(Multiply(Sine From Degrees((Event Player).scythe_angle), Facing Direction Of(Event Player)), Multiply(Cosine From Degrees((Event Player).scythe_angle), World Vector Of(Vector(-1, Multiply(0.3, (Event Player).scythe_swing), False), Event Player, Rotation))), (Event Player).scythe_length)), Add(World Vector Of(Vector(0, 1.2, 0), Event Player, Rotation And Translation), Multiply(Add(Multiply(Sine From Degrees(Add((Event Player).scythe_angle, 55)), Facing Direction Of(Event Player)), Multiply(Cosine From Degrees(Add((Event Player).scythe_angle, 55)), World Vector Of(Vector(-1, Multiply(0.3, (Event Player).scythe_swing), False), Event Player, Rotation))), (Event Player).scythe_length)), Team 1, Visible To Position and Radius);
                    Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, create_scroll, 2, True);
    }
}

rule ("potion of proficiency 1") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1)) > False;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Roadhog)));
            If(Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 3));
                Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1), 12);
                Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
            End;
        End;
        Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1), Subtract(Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1)), Value In Array((Event Player).potions, 5)));
    }
}
