rule ("spawn enemies subr") {
    event {
        Subroutine;
        spawn_enemies;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
        For Global Variable(i4, 0, Count Of(Global.enemy_ID_sequence), True);
            Set Global Variable(respawn_enemy, First Of(Filtered Array(All Dead Players(Team 1), (Current Array Element).enemy_ID)));
            If(And(Compare((Global.respawn_enemy).enemy_ID, ==, 5), Compare(Value In Array(Global.enemy_ID_sequence, Global.i4), <, 20)));
                Set Player Variable(Global.respawn_enemy, safeguard_fix, True);
                Teleport(Global.respawn_enemy, Global._extendedGlobalCollection);
                Start Forcing Player To Be Hero(Global.respawn_enemy, Hero(Brigitte));
                Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                Start Forcing Player To Be Hero(Global.respawn_enemy, Hero(Torbj√∂rn));
                Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
            End;
            Respawn(Global.respawn_enemy);
            Set Player Variable(Global.respawn_enemy, enemy_ID, Value In Array(Global.enemy_ID_sequence, Global.i4));
            Teleport(Global.respawn_enemy, Random Value In Array(Global.enemy_spawn));
            Set Player Variable(Global.respawn_enemy, safeguard_fix, False);
            Wait(0.3, Ignore Condition);
        End;
    }
}

rule ("enemy died") {
    event {
        Player Died;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).boss_ID == False;
    }
    actions {
        If(Or(Compare(Event Player, ==, Global.dialogue_bot), Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 4.4)));
            Resurrect(Event Player);
            Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
            Loop If(Is Dead(Event Player));
        Else;
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, nano, False);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, speed_boosted, False);
            If(Compare(Hero Of(Attacker), ==, Hero(Junkrat)));
                If(Array Contains((Attacker).scrolls_equip, 2));
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Sigma Accretion Impact Effect, Team 2, Eye Position(Event Player), 1);
                    Damage(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 6, Team 1, Surfaces), Attacker, 50);
                    Set Player Variable(Filtered Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 6, Team 1, Surfaces), Not(Has Status(Current Array Element, Phased Out))), electrify, 2);
                End;
            End;
            If(Array Contains(All Players(Team 2), Attacker));
                If(Not(Global.first_kill));
                    Set Global Variable(first_kill, True);
                End;
                If(Not(Array Contains(Array(5, 6, 7, 14, 15, 16, 26), Global.phase)));
                    If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 8));
                        Modify Player Variable(All Players(Team 2), euros, Add, 100);
                        Modify Global Variable(euros_total, Add, 100);
                    Else If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 9));
                        Modify Player Variable(All Players(Team 2), euros, Add, 150);
                        Modify Global Variable(euros_total, Add, 150);
                    Else;
                        Modify Player Variable(All Players(Team 2), euros, Add, 10);
                        Modify Global Variable(euros_total, Add, 10);
                    End;
                End;
            End;
            If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 10));
                Clear Status(Event Player, Unkillable);
                Modify Player Variable(All Players(Team 2), euros, Add, 50);
                Modify Global Variable(euros_total, Add, 50);
            End;
            Destroy Effect(First Of((Event Player).trail));
            Destroy In-World Text(Value In Array((Event Player).trail, True));
            Destroy Effect(Value In Array((Event Player).trail, 2));
            Destroy Icon(Value In Array((Event Player).trail, 3));
            Wait(0.03, Ignore Condition);
            If(Compare((Global.reaper).death_mark, ==, Event Player));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_received, Subtract(130, Multiply(15, Global.difficulty)));
                Set Damage Received(Event Player, Multiply((Event Player).damage_received, If-Then-Else((Event Player).nano, 1.5, 1)));
                Set Player Variable(Global.reaper, death_mark, Null);
    }
}

rule ("bot strafe") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, strafe, True);
        While(True);
            Modify Player Variable(Event Player, strafe, Multiply, -1);
            Wait(Random Real(0.25, If-Then-Else(Or(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 2), (Event Player).speed_boosted), 1, 1.5)), Ignore Condition);
        End;
    }
}

rule ("bot pause") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, throttle_mag, If-Then-Else((Event Player).speed_boosted, True, Not((Event Player).throttle_mag)));
        Wait(Random Real(1, 3), Ignore Condition);
        Loop;
    }
}

rule ("enemy throttle") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).enemy_ID != False;
        (Event Player).start_pathfind == False;
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(0.1, Abort When False);
        If(Or(Array Contains(Array(2, 3, 5), (Event Player).enemy_ID), And(Array Contains(Array(21, 23, 24, 25), (Event Player).enemy_ID), Compare(Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire)), <=, False))));
            If(Array Contains(Array(3, 23), (Event Player).enemy_ID));
                Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, Add(Multiply(Direction Towards(Event Player, (Event Player).target), If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), >, 16), 1, If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), <, 14), -1, Null))), Multiply(World Vector Of(Left, Event Player, Rotation), (Event Player).strafe)), (Event Player).throttle_mag, To World, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 24));
                Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, Add(Multiply(Direction Towards(Event Player, (Event Player).target), If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), >, 8), 1, If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), <, 6), -1, Null))), Multiply(World Vector Of(Left, Event Player, Rotation), (Event Player).strafe)), (Event Player).throttle_mag, To World, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
            Else;
                Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, Add(Multiply(Direction Towards(Event Player, (Event Player).target), If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), >, 10), 1, If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), <, 8), -1, Null))), Multiply(World Vector Of(Left, Event Player, Rotation), (Event Player).strafe)), (Event Player).throttle_mag, To World, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
            End;
        Else;
            Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, Add(Direction Towards(Event Player, (Event Player).target), Multiply(Multiply(World Vector Of(Left, Event Player, Rotation), (Event Player).strafe), 0.4)), Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), >, 2), To World, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
    }
}

rule ("instant target switch") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Is Dead((Event Player).target) == True;
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Abort If((Event Player).hex);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, target, First Of(Sorted Array(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), And(Or(Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element)), (Current Array Element).zomnic), Not((Current Array Element).is_downed))), Add(Add(Distance Between(Event Player, Current Array Element), Multiply(1000, Not(Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position(Current Array Element), Barriers Do Not Block LOS)))), Multiply(1000, Compare(Vertical Angle From Direction(Direction Towards(Event Player, Current Array Element)), <, -50))))));
    }
}

rule ("v/instakillager start hammering") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Torbj√∂rn;
    }
    conditions {
        Array Contains(Array(1, 7), (Event Player).enemy_ID) == True;
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), <, 2.5));
            Start Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire));
            While(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), <, 3));
                Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
            End;
            Stop Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire));
        End;
        Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("k/sp/sk/over/overoverkillager attack") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Torbj√∂rn;
    }
    conditions {
        Array Contains(Array(2, 3, 5, 8, 9), (Event Player).enemy_ID) == True;
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;

    actions {
        If(Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Event Player).target), Barriers Do Not Block LOS));
            If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 3));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, real, 1.7);
                Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, real, False, True, None);
                Wait(1.7, Ignore Condition);
            End;
            Press Button(Event Player, If-Then-Else(Or(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 8), And(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 9), Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), <, 7))), Button(Secondary Fire), Button(Primary Fire)));
            Wait(If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 5), Random Real(1, 2), Random Real(If-Then-Else(Array Contains(Array(8, 9), (Event Player).enemy_ID), 1.1, 0.6), 1.5)), Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

                    Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 2));

            End;
        End;
        Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("gri/chi/chernobyllager explode") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Torbj√∂rn;
    }
    conditions {
        Array Contains(Array(4, 6, 10), (Event Player).enemy_ID) == True;
        (Event Player).grillager_activate == True;
        Or(Is Dead(Event Player), Not(Is Using Ability 2(Event Player))) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, grillager_victims, Filtered Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 10), 12, 5), Team 2, Surfaces), And(Is Alive(Current Array Element), Not(Has Status(Current Array Element, Phased Out)))));
        If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 4));
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ashe Dynamite Explosion Effect, Color(Orange), Eye Position(Event Player), 5);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ashe Dynamite Explosion Sound, Color(White), Eye Position(Event Player), 200);
            Set Player Variable((Event Player).grillager_victims, burner, True);
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 6));
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Pharah Concussive Blast Effect, Team 2, Eye Position(Event Player), 5);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Winston Jump Pack Landing Effect, Team 2, Eye Position(Event Player), 5);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Sigma Hypersphere Implosion Sound, Color(White), Eye Position(Event Player), 200);
        Else;
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), DVa Self Destruct Explosion Sound, Color(White), Eye Position(Event Player), 200);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), DVa Self Destruct Explosion Sound, Color(White), Eye Position(Event Player), 200);
            Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Doomfist Meteor Strike Impact Effect, Team 1, Eye Position(Event Player), 1);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Explosion, Color(Green), Eye Position(Event Player), 10);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Explosion, Color(Green), Eye Position(Event Player), 15);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion, Color(Green), Eye Position(Event Player), 20);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion, Color(Green), Eye Position(Event Player), 25);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, falloff_pos, Eye Position(Event Player));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, falloff, 10);
            Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring, Color(Green), (Event Player).falloff_pos, (Event Player).falloff, Visible To Position and Radius);
            Modify Player Variable(Event Player, falloff_effect, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
            Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Aura, Color(Green), (Event Player).falloff_pos, (Event Player).falloff, Visible To Position and Radius);
            Modify Player Variable(Event Player, falloff_effect, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
        End;
        For Player Variable(Event Player, i, 0, Count Of((Event Player).grillager_victims), True);
            Damage(Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i)), Null, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 10), Multiply(125, Subtract(16, Distance Between(Event Player, Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i))))), Multiply(Divide(Add(40, Multiply(15, Global.difficulty)), 5), Subtract(6, Distance Between(Event Player, Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i)))))));
            If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 4));
                Set Status(Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i)), Null, Burning, 3.5);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 6));
                Set Status(Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i)), Null, Frozen, 3);
            End;
            Apply Impulse(Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i)), Add(Direction Towards(Event Player, Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i))), Vector(0, 0.7, 0)), If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 10), 20, 14), To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
            Set Player Variable(Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i)), took_knockback, 1);
            Chase Player Variable At Rate(Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i)), took_knockback, False, True, Destination and Rate);
        End;
        Wait(Multiply(0.05, Is Dead(Event Player)), Ignore Condition);
        Teleport(Event Player, Global.compressBakeMatcher);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, grillager_activate, False);
    }
}

rule ("chi/chernobyllager explode") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Torbj√∂rn;
    }
    conditions {
        Array Contains(Array(6, 10), (Event Player).enemy_ID) == True;
        (Event Player).grillager_activate == False;
    }
    actions {
        If(Or(If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 10), And(Compare(Health(Event Player), <=, True), Is Alive(Event Player)), Is Dead(Event Player)), And(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), <, 3), Not((Event Player).has_status))));
            If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 10));
                Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ultimate));
                Stop Throttle In Direction(Event Player);
                Wait(1.5, Ignore Condition);
            End;
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, grillager_activate, True);
        End;
        Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).falloff >= 10;

            Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, falloff, False, 10, None);
        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, falloff);
        While(Compare((Event Player).falloff_effect, !=, Empty Array));
            Destroy Effect(First Of((Event Player).falloff_effect));
            Modify Player Variable(Event Player, falloff_effect, Remove From Array By Index, False);
        End;
    }
}

rule ("overkillager turret deploy") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Torbj√∂rn;
    }
    conditions {
        Array Contains(Array(8, 9), (Event Player).enemy_ID) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(Random Real(4, 8), Ignore Condition);
        Abort If Condition Is False;
        If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 9));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, random, Random Integer(Not((Event Player).random), 2));
            If((Event Player).random);
                Set Projectile Gravity(Event Player, 1000000);
                Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
                Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
            Else;
                Set Projectile Gravity(Event Player, 15);
                While(Not(Is Using Ultimate(Event Player)));
                    Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, 100);
                    Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ultimate));
                    Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                End;
            End;
            While(Is Using Ultimate(Event Player));
                Press Button(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire));
                Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
            End;
        Else;
            Set Projectile Gravity(Event Player, 1000000);
            Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
            Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Set Projectile Gravity(Event Player, 100);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).enemy_ID == 24;
        (Event Player).has_status == False;
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;

        Wait(True, Abort When False);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, safeguard_fix, True);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, max_health, Health(Event Player));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location, Position Of(Event Player));
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Start Forcing Player To Be Hero(Event Player, Hero(Torbj√∂rn));
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Start Forcing Player To Be Hero(Event Player, Hero(Brigitte));
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Set Player Health(Event Player, (Event Player).max_health);
        Teleport(Event Player, (Event Player).boss_target_location);
        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, safeguard_fix, False);
    }
}

rule ("boss throttle") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Array Contains(Array(1, 4), (Event Player).boss_ID) == True;
        (Event Player).pre_init == False;
        (Event Player).start_pathfind == False;
        (Event Player).avoid_enviro == False;
        (Event Player).attack == False;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 1));
            Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, Add(Multiply(Direction Towards(Event Player, (Event Player).target), If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), >, 10), 1, If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), <, 8), -1, Null))), Multiply(World Vector Of(Left, Event Player, Rotation), (Event Player).strafe)), 1, To World, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 4));
            Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, Direction Towards(Event Player, (Event Player).target), Multiply(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), >, 2), (Event Player).rein_throttle_mag), To World, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
    }
}

rule ("genji init") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Genji;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 5;
        (Event Player).boss_ID == 1;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, pre_init, False);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, turn_rate, 1000);
        Set Move Speed(Event Player, 70);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_dealt, Add(30, Multiply(10, Global.difficulty)));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_received, Subtract(130, Multiply(15, Global.difficulty)));
        Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_dealt);
        Set Damage Received(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_received);
        Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Event Player).target)), (Event Player).turn_rate, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
        Create Dummy Bot(Hero(Reinhardt), Team 1, -1, Position Of(Event Player), Facing Direction Of(Event Player));
        Set Player Variable(Last Created Entity, boss_ID, 1.2);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_pet, Last Created Entity);
        Create Dummy Bot(Hero(Genji), Team 1, -1, Global._extendedGlobalCollection, Null);
        Set Player Variable(Last Created Entity, boss_ID, 1.1);
        Modify Player Variable(Event Player, boss_pet, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        Clear Status(Event Player, Phased Out);
        Destroy Effect((Event Player).effects);
    }
}

rule ("genji no enviro death") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Genji;
    }
    conditions {
        Y Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)) <= 2.5;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, start_pathfind, False);
        Set Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Vector(14, 80, -64.7)), To World);
        Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, Direction Towards(Event Player, Vector(14, 20, -64.7)), 1, To World, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
        Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Vector(13.991, 80, -64.698)), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
        Start Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Jump));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, avoid_enviro, True);
        While(Is In Air(Event Player));
            While(Compare(Y Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)), <, 3));
                Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
                Apply Impulse(Event Player, Up, 3, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
                Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
            End;
            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Event Player).target)), (Event Player).turn_rate, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
        Stop Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Jump));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, avoid_enviro, False);
    }
}

rule ("genji special attack") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Genji;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 5;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(Random Real(3, 5), Ignore Condition);
        While(Or(Is Using Ability 2(Event Player), Not(Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Event Player).target), Barriers Do Not Block LOS))));
            Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        If(And(Not((Event Player).boss_phase), Compare(Normalized Health(Event Player), <, 0.5)));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, attack, 4);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_phase, True);
        Else;
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, attack, Random Integer(If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), <, 11), 1, 3), If-Then-Else((Event Player).boss_phase, 4, 3)));
        End;
        Wait Until(Not((Event Player).attack), 99999);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        End;

rule ("boss death") {
    event {
        Player Died;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Array Contains(Array(1, 5), (Event Player).boss_ID) == True;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 5));
            Set Player Variable(All Players(Team 2), euros, 6969);
            Set Global Variable(euros_total, 6969);
            Set Player Variable(All Players(Team 2), real, 1337);
            Set Global Variable(real_total, 1337);
            Set Global Variable(sombra_egg, 69);
            Wait(2, Ignore Condition);
            Teleport(All Players(Team 2), Global.map);
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Sombra Translocator Disappear Sound, Team 1, Global.map, 200);
            Small Message(All Players(Team 2), Custom String("Some new dialogue has been unlocked."));
            Wait(3, Ignore Condition);
            Small Message(All Players(Team 2), Custom String("Avoid skipping cutscenes to see them!"));
            Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
            Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, Slot Of(Event Player));
        Else;
            Set Global Variable(phase, 6);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, attack, 5);
            Set Global Variable(objective_complete, True);
            Modify Player Variable(All Players(Team 2), euros, Add, 300);
            Modify Global Variable(euros_total, Add, 300);
            Modify Player Variable(All Players(Team 2), real, Add, 100);
            Modify Global Variable(real_total, Add, 100);
    }
}

rule ("objective colour subr") {
    event {
        Subroutine;
        obj_color;
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(obj_color_r, 255);
        Set Global Variable(obj_color_g, 255);
        Set Global Variable(obj_color_b, 255);
        Stop Chasing Global Variable(obj_color_r);
        Stop Chasing Global Variable(obj_color_g);
        Stop Chasing Global Variable(obj_color_b);
        Wait(0.03, Ignore Condition);
        For Global Variable(i3, 0, 3, True);
            Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
            Set Global Variable(obj_color_g, Null);
            Set Global Variable(obj_color_b, Null);
            Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
            Set Global Variable(obj_color_g, 255);
            Set Global Variable(obj_color_b, 255);
        End;
        Wait(0.4, Ignore Condition);
        While(True);
            Chase Global Variable Over Time(obj_color_r, 255, 1.3, Destination and Duration);
            Chase Global Variable Over Time(obj_color_g, 120, 1.3, Destination and Duration);
            Chase Global Variable Over Time(obj_color_b, 255, 1.3, Destination and Duration);
            Wait(1.3, Ignore Condition);
            Chase Global Variable Over Time(obj_color_r, 150, 1.3, Destination and Duration);
            Chase Global Variable Over Time(obj_color_g, 30, 1.3, Destination and Duration);
            Chase Global Variable Over Time(obj_color_b, 255, 1.3, Destination and Duration);
            Wait(1.3, Ignore Condition);
        End;
    }
}

        End;
    }

rule ("objective completed ding") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.objective_complete == True;
        Global.phase > 0.5;
    }
    actions {
        Big Message(All Players(Team 2), Random Value In Array(Append To Array(Array(Custom String("Bewitching success!"), Custom String("Junktastic success!"), Custom String("Monstrous success!"), Custom String("Reapalicious success!")), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.sombra_egg, ==, 69), Custom String("Sucesso incr√≠vel!"), Empty Array))));
        For Global Variable(i6, 0, 4, True);
            Play Effect(Players In Slot(Evaluate Once(Global.i6), Team 2), Buff Impact Sound, Color(White), Players In Slot(Evaluate Once(Global.i6), Team 2), 200);
        End;
    }
}

rule ("skip cutscene") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.main_dialogue != Null;
        Y Component Of(Global.skip_cutscene_pos) < 100;
        Is True For All(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element))), Compare(Distance Between(Current Array Element, Global.skip_cutscene_pos), <, 2.3)) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, True);
        Wait Until(Not(Global.main_dialogue), 99999);
        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, False);
    }
}

rule ("return cam") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.return_cam == True;
    }
    actions {
        Chase Player Variable Over Time(Event Player, cutscene_cam_pos, Eye Position(Event Player), True, Destination and Duration);
        Chase Player Variable Over Time(Event Player, cutscene_cam_lookat, Add(Eye Position(Event Player), Facing Direction Of(Event Player)), True, Destination and Duration);
        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        Stop Camera(Event Player);
        Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, cutscene_cam_pos);
        Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, cutscene_cam_lookat);
        Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, cutscene_cam_speedup);
    }
}

rule ("in spawn check") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase < 11;
        Dot Product(Vector Towards(First Of(Global.spawn_corners), Vector(X Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)), False, Z Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)))), Global.spawn_line) > False;
        Dot Product(Vector Towards(First Of(Global.spawn_corners), Vector(X Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)), False, Z Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)))), Global.spawn_line) < Raise To Power(Magnitude Of(Global.spawn_line), 2);
        Multiply(Dot Product(Vector Towards(First Of(Global.spawn_corners), Vector(X Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)), False, Z Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)))), Normalize(Cross Product(Global.spawn_line, Down))), 50) > False;
        Multiply(Dot Product(Vector Towards(First Of(Global.spawn_corners), Vector(X Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)), False, Z Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)))), Normalize(Cross Product(Global.spawn_line, Down))), 50) < 2500;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, in_spawn, True);
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, in_spawn, False);
        If(Is Dummy Bot(Event Player));
            Set Global Variable(_objectVariable_0, True);
            Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, True);
            Wait Until(Not(Global.main_dialogue), 99999);
            Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, False);
    }
}

rule ("stuck in spawn phase 0") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).in_spawn == False;
        Global.phase < True;
        Is Dummy Bot(Event Player) == False;
    }
    actions {
        Apply Impulse(Event Player, Direction From Angles(Horizontal Angle From Direction(Direction Towards(Event Player, Vector(-12.838, 7.257, -0.748))), -30), 5, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
        Wait(0.25, Abort When False);
        Respawn(Event Player);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Tracer Recall Reappear Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 100);
        Small Message(Event Player, Custom String("You cannot yet leave spawn."));
    }
}

rule ("phase 1+ cannot re-enter spawn") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).in_spawn == True;
        Global.phase > 0.5;
    }
    actions {
        If((Event Player).egg);
            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
            If(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, Vector(0.952, 6.1, 1.055)), <, 7));
                Teleport(Event Player, Vector(0.952, 6.1, 1.055));
            Else If(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, Vector(-26.711, 1.1, -0.393)), <, 7));
                Teleport(Event Player, Vector(-26.711, 1.1, -0.393));
            Else;
                Teleport(Event Player, Vector(-12.008, 0.44, -8.068));
            End;
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Tracer Recall Reappear Sound, Color(White), Event Player, 100);
        End;
        Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
        If(Compare((Event Player).egg, ==, 1));
            Small Message(Event Player, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.phase, ==, 9), Custom String("This is not where you are looking for."), Custom String("You can no longer return to the spawn room.")));
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).egg, ==, 31));
            Small Message(Event Player, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.phase, ==, 9), Custom String("Ahem. I said this is not where you are looking for."), Custom String("Ahem. I said you cannot return to the spawn room.")));
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).egg, ==, 61));
            Small Message(Event Player, Custom String("What are you trying to achieve here?"));
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).egg, ==, 91));
            Small Message(Event Player, Custom String("Is this fun for you? Do you find this fun? What is wrong with you?"));
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).egg, ==, 121));
            Small Message(Event Player, Custom String("You must really like that warping sound."));
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).egg, ==, 161));
            Start Rule(egg, Do Nothing);
        End;
        Modify Player Variable(Event Player, egg, Add, 1);
    }
}

rule ("first cutscene") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == False;
        Or(Compare(Global._objectVariable_0, ==, 1), Is True For All(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element))), Has Spawned(Current Array Element))) == True;
        Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element))) != Empty Array;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(True, Abort When False);
        Set Global Variable(phase, 0.1);
        Set Global Variable(objective_complete, True);
        Set Global Variable(skip_cutscene_pos, Vector(-12.386, 2.259, -4.887));
        If(Not(Global._objectVariable_0));
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("Our tale begins in Adlersbrunn, where the lord of the castle has called for heroes to come to his aid,"), 0.5), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("to defend him against the mad Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein and his minions."), 1), Array(Hero(Mercy), Custom String("Excuse me, minion? Tch, don't be absurd. If anything, the mad doctor is my minion."), 1), Array(Hero(Junkrat), Custom String("Oh, stick a sock in it, you old hag. I'll have ya know the great Dr.‚Äã Junkenstein doesn't take kindly to such remarks."), 1), Array(Hero(Mercy), Custom String("Old- old hag!? Why, I never!"), 1), Array(Hero(Roadhog), Custom String("To be fair, you're somewhere between three to six centuries old."), 1), Array(Hero(Mercy), Custom String("Yet with the complexion of a rose! It's no easy feat staying so youthful."), 1), Array(Hero(Mercy), Custom String("Do you know how much I spend on vitamin C serums alone?"), 1), Array(Hero(Reaper), Custom String("My wife left me."), 1.5)));
            Call Subroutine(main_dialogue);
        End;
        Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
        If(Global._objectVariable_0);
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("........."), 1), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("...What are you doing with Zommy. Put her back."), 1), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("She's sensitive to the moonlight."), 1)));
            Call Subroutine(main_dialogue);
            Wait(1, Ignore Condition);
            Kill(Global.faq_bot, Null);
            Wait(2, Ignore Condition);
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("...Okay, nevermind. Let's just move on."), 1), Array(Hero(Reaper), Custom String("I miss my wife."), 1.5)));
            Call Subroutine(main_dialogue);
        End;
        Set Global Variable(skip_cutscene_pos, Global._extendedGlobalCollection);
        Set Global Variable(phase, 1);
        Set Global Variable(objective, Custom String("Reach the Village of Adlersbrunn."));
        Start Rule(obj_color, Restart Rule);
        Set Global Variable(objective_pos, Vector(8.302, 6, -68.151));
        Set Global Variable(objective_complete, False);
        Set Player Variable(All Players(Team 2), late_join_check, True);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 2, 5);
    }
}

    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {

        Is Dummy Bot(Event Player) == False;

    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, in_boundary, True);
        Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);

    }

rule ("phase 3 spawning event") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 3;
        Global.objective_value == False;
        Number Of Living Players(Team 1) <= 3;
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(objective_value, 0.5);
        Set Global Variable(enemy_ID_sequence, Array(1, 1, 2, 2));
        Call Subroutine(spawn_enemies);
        Wait Until(Compare(Number Of Living Players(Team 1), <=, 3), 99999);
        Set Global Variable(enemy_ID_sequence, Array(1, 2, 2));
        Call Subroutine(spawn_enemies);
        Wait Until(Compare(Number Of Living Players(Team 1), <=, 3), 99999);
        Set Global Variable(enemy_ID_sequence, Array(If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 3, 1), 2, 1, 4));
        Call Subroutine(spawn_enemies);
        Wait Until(Compare(Number Of Living Players(Team 1), <=, 3), 99999);
        Set Global Variable(enemy_ID_sequence, Array(1, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 6, 4), 2, 3, 4));
        Call Subroutine(spawn_enemies);
        Wait Until(Compare(Number Of Living Players(Team 1), <=, 2), 99999);
        Set Global Variable(enemy_ID_sequence, Array(If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 7, 1), 2, 2, 3, 4, 8));
        Call Subroutine(spawn_enemies);
        Set Global Variable(objective_value, 9);
    }
}

rule ("end of slaughter + genji intro cutscene") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 3;
        Global.objective_value == 9;
        Global.dialogue_priority < 3;
        Number Of Living Players(Team 1) == 1;
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(phase, 4);
        Set Global Variable(objective_complete, True);
        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        Abort If(Compare(Global.dialogue_priority, >=, 3));
        Set Global Variable(skip_cutscene_pos, Vector(16.597, 7.058, -68.525));
        Set Global Variable(dialogue_priority, 2);
        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, True);
        Wait Until(Not(Global.main_dialogue), 99999);
        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, False);
        Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Mercy), Custom String("My, my, I haven't felt such fun since the genocide of the Western Shelf sixty moons ago!"), 1), Array(Hero(Reaper), Custom String("I haven't felt happy since 2016."), 1), Array(Hero(Junkrat), Custom String("Ahahahahaha! Oh, this bloodshed's got me mighty stoked. What a blast. "), 1), Array(Hero(Junkrat), Custom String("What were we doing again?"), 1), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("As the dust settled from the massacre, one hero emerged from the darkness."), 1.5)));
        Call Subroutine(main_dialogue);
        Set Global Variable(dialogue_priority, False);
        Set Global Variable(skip_cutscene_pos, Global._extendedGlobalCollection);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, 5);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, 6);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, 7);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, 8);
        Set Slow Motion(20);
        Set Global Variable(no_hud, True);
        Create Dummy Bot(Hero(Genji), Team 1, -1, Vector(-2.233, 24.45, -72.894), Vector(2.611, 0.5, 1.146));
        Set Global Variable(boss, Last Created Entity);
        Set Player Variable(Last Created Entity, pre_init, True);
        Set Player Variable(Last Created Entity, boss_ID, 1);
        Wait(1.8, Ignore Condition);
        Set Slow Motion(100);
        Set Global Variable(return_cam, True);
        Start Facing(Global.boss, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Global.boss), Eye Position((Global.boss).target)), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);

rule ("regrouped after merchant") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 8;
        Y Component Of(Global.objective_pos) < 100;
        Is True For All(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element))), Compare(Distance Between(Current Array Element, Global.objective_pos), <, 4)) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(enemy_spawn_2, Global.enemy_spawn);
        Set Global Variable(phase, 9);
        Set Global Variable(boundary_corners, Array(Vector(103.485, 13.9, -66.421), Vector(74.555, 13.9, -59.152)));
        Set Global Variable(objective_pos, Vector(77.842, 13.935, -98.146));
        Set Global Variable(boundary_line, Vector Towards(First Of(Global.boundary_corners), Last Of(Global.boundary_corners)));
        Start Rule(delete_bound_effects, Restart Rule);
        Press Button(Global.merchant, Button(Ability 1));
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, Slot Of((Global.merchant).attack));
        Set Global Variable(shop_open, False);
        Wait(0.4, Ignore Condition);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 2, 9);
        Stop Chasing Global Variable(shop_angle);
    }
}

        Ongoing - Global;
    }

        Global.phase == 9;

    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable At Index(scripted_spawns, 2, True);
        For Global Variable(i4, 0, 4, True);
            Set Global Variable(enemy_spawn, Value In Array(Array(Vector(54.223, 7.977, -74.398), Vector(54.646, 12.977, -73.179), Vector(40.486, 11.923, -97.597), Vector(50.089, 9.807, -85.586)), Global.i4));
            Create Dummy Bot(If-Then-Else(Modulo(Global.i4, 2), Hero(Torbj√∂rn), Hero(Brigitte)), Team 1, Add(Global.i4, 5), Global.enemy_spawn, Up);
            Set Player Variable(Last Created Entity, enemy_ID, Value In Array(Array(21, 2, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 23, 21), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 3, 2)), Global.i4));
            Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
        End;
    }
}

rule ("phase 11 spawning event") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase >= 11;
        Global.phase < 13;
        Global.dragon_blood_cache != Global.dragon_blood_qty;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Set Global Variable(dragon_blood_cache, Global.dragon_blood_qty);
        Start Rule(phase_11_spawn, Restart Rule);
    }
}

rule ("collect blood") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 11;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare(Global.hint, >, True));
            If(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, First Of(Sorted Array(Global.dragon_blood_actual_spawn, Distance Between(Event Player, Current Array Element)))), <, 1.5));
                If(Array Contains(Array(1, 1.9), Global.mercy_drop));
                    If(Not((Event Player).no_pickup));
                        Small Message(Event Player, Custom String("You cannot pick this up during a cutscene."));
                        Set Player Variable(Event Player, no_pickup, True);
                    End;
                Else;
                    Set Global Variable(hint, Null);
                    Chase Global Variable At Rate(hint, 60, True, Destination and Rate);
                    Set Global Variable(last_collected_blood, Event Player);
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, blood_collected, Index Of Array Value(Global.dragon_blood_actual_spawn, First Of(Sorted Array(Global.dragon_blood_actual_spawn, Distance Between(Event Player, Current Array Element)))));
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Pickup Effect, Color(Red), Value In Array(Global.dragon_blood_actual_spawn, (Event Player).blood_collected), 1);
                    Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                    Set Global Variable At Index(dragon_blood_actual_spawn, (Event Player).blood_collected, Global._extendedGlobalCollection);
                    Modify Global Variable(dragon_blood_qty, Subtract, 1);
                    Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                    Small Message(Remove From Array(All Players(All Teams), Event Player), Custom String("{0} collected a bottle of dragon's blood.", Event Player));
                    Small Message(Event Player, Custom String("You collected a bottle of dragon's blood."));
                    If(Not(Global.dragon_blood_qty));
                        Set Global Variable(objective_complete, True);
                        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
                        Abort If(Compare(Global.dialogue_priority, >=, 3));
                        Set Global Variable(dialogue_priority, 2);
                        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, True);
                        Wait Until(Not(Global.main_dialogue), 99999);
                        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, False);
                        Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reaper), Custom String("Now let's head back to the bridge. We'll perform the ritual there."), 1.5)));
                        Call Subroutine(main_dialogue);
                        Set Global Variable(dialogue_priority, False);
                        Set Global Variable(phase, 12);
                        Start Rule(obj_color, Restart Rule);
                        Set Global Variable(objective_complete, False);
                        Set Global Variable(objective, Custom String("Perform the ritual at the bridge."));
                        Destroy Icon(Global.dragon_blood_hint_icon);
                        While(Compare(Global.dragon_blood_effects, !=, Empty Array));
                            Destroy Effect(First Of(Global.dragon_blood_effects));
                            Modify Global Variable(dragon_blood_effects, Remove From Array By Index, False);
                            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                        End;
                    Else;
                        Start Rule(obj_color, Restart Rule);
                        Set Global Variable(objective, Custom String("Collect {0} {1} of dragon's blood.", Global.dragon_blood_qty, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.dragon_blood_qty, >, True), Custom String("bottles"), Custom String("bottle"))));
                    End;
                    If(Not(Global.mercy_drop));
                        Start Rule(mercy_drop_blood, Do Nothing);
                    End;
                End;
            End;
        End;
        Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

        Subroutine;
        mercy_drop_blood;

One must have a tender, trained touch to handle such a precious item."), 1), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("The Witch, upon receiving the bottle, immediately dropped it, spilling it all over her robe."), 1), Array(Hero(Mercy), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.sombra_egg, ==, 69), Custom String("‚Ä®MONTE DE MERDA! SON OF A GODFORSAKEN, CURSED MOTHERFU-"), Custom String("‚Ä®VERDAMMTE SCHEI√üE! SON OF A GODFORSAKEN, CURSED MOTHERFU-")), 0.2), Array(Hero(Junkrat), Custom String("Woah, woah! Watch the language, swiss cheese! My Monster here is literally a minor!"), 1), Array(Hero(Roadhog), Custom String("I'm also neurodivergent."), 1.5)));

rule ("brig mace no knockback") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Brigitte;
    }
    conditions {
        Is Using Ability 1(Event Player) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Knockback Dealt(Event Player, 0);
        Wait Until(Not(Is Using Ability 1(Event Player)), 1);
        Set Knockback Dealt(Event Player, 200);
    }
}

    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.mercy_drop == 1;
        Global.line_number == 2;
        Global.phase == 11;
        Global.letter_scroll >= 50;

    actions {
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ana Biotic Grenade Explosion Sound, Team 1, Eye Position(If-Then-Else(Compare(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), !=, Empty Array), First Of(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2)), Random Value In Array(All Players(Team 2)))), 200);
        Small Message(Filtered Array(All Players(All Teams), Compare(Hero Of(Current Array Element), !=, Hero(Mercy))), Custom String("{0} dropped a bottle of dragon's blood.", If-Then-Else(Is Hero Being Played(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), First Of(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2)), Custom String("The Witch"))));
        Small Message(Players On Hero(Hero(Mercy), Team 2), Custom String("You dropped a bottle of dragon's blood."));
        Wait Until(Compare(Global.line_number, ==, 3), 20);
        Abort If(Compare(Global.mercy_drop, ==, 2));
        Set Global Variable(mercy_drop, 1.9);
    }
}

rule ("junkrat faster mines") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        Junkrat;
    }
    conditions {
        Ability Charge(Event Player, Button(Ability 1)) < 2;
        Value In Array((Event Player).potions, 5) > False;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(Subtract(8, Value In Array((Event Player).potions, 5)), Abort When False);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, mine_cache, Ability Charge(Event Player, Button(Ability 1)));
        Set Ability Charge(Event Player, Button(Ability 1), 2);
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Set Ability Charge(Event Player, Button(Ability 1), Add((Event Player).mine_cache, True));
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("phase 14 spawning event") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 14;
        Number Of Living Players(Team 1) <= 4;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(Random Real(3, 6), Abort When False);
        Set Global Variable(enemy_ID_sequence, Array(Random Value In Array(Array(2, 3, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 7, 4), 6)), Random Value In Array(Array(2, 3, 4, 6))));
        Call Subroutine(spawn_enemies);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("shop stocks randomize") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.shop_open == True;
        Is Dummy Bot(Event Player) == False;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, random, Append To Array(Sorted Array(Array Slice(Randomized Array(Global.numbers), False, 3), Current Array Element), 10));
        For Player Variable(Event Player, i, 0, Count Of((Event Player).random), True);
            Modify Player Variable At Index(Event Player, potions_max, (Event Player).i, Add, Subtract(Value In Array((Event Player).random, (Event Player).i), Value In Array((Event Player).random, Subtract((Event Player).i, True))));
        End;
        Modify Player Variable At Index(Event Player, potions_max, 4, Add, Random Integer(2, 5));
        Modify Player Variable At Index(Event Player, potions_max, 5, Add, Random Integer(True, Min(3, Subtract(4, Value In Array((Event Player).potions_max, 5)))));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, random, Random Integer(False, 5));
        Modify Player Variable At Index(Event Player, potions_max, 6, Add, (Event Player).random);
        Modify Player Variable At Index(Event Player, potions_max, 7, Add, Subtract(5, (Event Player).random));
        Modify Player Variable At Index(Event Player, potions_max, 8, Add, 1);
    }
}

rule ("cowboy init") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Cassidy;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 14;
        (Event Player).boss_ID == 2;
    }
    actions {
        Create Beam Effect(If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).trail, >, False), All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Zarya Particle Beam, World Vector Of(Up, Event Player, Rotation And Translation), Add(World Vector Of(Up, Event Player, Rotation And Translation), Multiply(Vector Towards(World Vector Of(Up, Event Player, Rotation And Translation), (Event Player).trail_cache), (Event Player).trail)), Team 1, Visible To Position and Radius);
        Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, Multiply(Direction Towards(Event Player, First Of((Event Player).pos_cache)), If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, First Of((Event Player).pos_cache)), >, True), 1, (Event Player).strafe)), 1, To World, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, avoid_enviro, True);
        Set Global Variable(cowboy_tp_array, Array(Vector(56.67, 22.931, -104.653), Vector(82.514, 21.407, -64.821), Vector(96.779, 17.066, -74.286), Vector(62.23, 18.978, -92.354), Vector(83.269, 13.141, -102.456), Vector(70.765, 13.565, -76.652)));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, pos_cache, Position Of(Event Player));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, pre_init, False);
        Set Projectile Gravity(Event Player, 200);
        Set Projectile Speed(Event Player, False);
        Set Move Speed(Event Player, 100);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_dealt, Add(30, Multiply(10, Global.difficulty)));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_received, Subtract(130, Multiply(15, Global.difficulty)));
        Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_dealt);
        Set Damage Received(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_received);
        Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Add(Add(Eye Position((Event Player).target), Vector(0, -0.5, 0)), Vector(Random Real(-0.8, 0.8), False, Random Real(-0.8, 0.8)))), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
        Create Dummy Bot(Hero(Ashe), Team 1, -1, Position Of(Event Player), Facing Direction Of(Event Player));
        Set Player Variable(Last Created Entity, boss_ID, 2.1);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_pet, Last Created Entity);
        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, pos_cache, True, Random Value In Array(Remove From Array(Global.cowboy_tp_array, (Event Player).pos_cache)));
        Call Subroutine(cowboy_tp);
        Clear Status(Event Player, Phased Out);
    }
}

    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Cassidy;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 14;
        (Event Player).attack < 3;
    }

        Wait(Random Real(0.6, 1.5), Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("cowboy tp") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Cassidy;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 14;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(Random Real(4, 8), Ignore Condition);
        Wait Until(Not((Event Player).attack), 15);
        Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, pos_cache, True, Random Value In Array(Remove From Array(Global.cowboy_tp_array, (Event Player).pos_cache)));
        Call Subroutine(cowboy_tp);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("cowboy too far from pos cache") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Cassidy;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 14;
    }
    actions {
        If(Or(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, First Of((Event Player).pos_cache)), >, 5), Compare(Y Component Of(Eye Position(Event Player)), <, Y Component Of(First Of((Event Player).pos_cache)))));
            Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
            If(Or(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, First Of((Event Player).pos_cache)), >, 5), Compare(Y Component Of(Eye Position(Event Player)), <, Y Component Of(First Of((Event Player).pos_cache)))));
                Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, Add(Multiply(Direction Towards(Event Player, (Event Player).target), If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), >, 16), 1, If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target), <, 14), -1, Null))), Multiply(World Vector Of(Left, Event Player, Rotation), (Event Player).strafe)), 1, To World, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
                While(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, First Of((Event Player).pos_cache)), >, 2.5));
                    Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
                End;
            End;
        End;
        Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("cowboy tp no envirokill/in spawn") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Cassidy;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 14;
        Or(Compare(Y Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)), <, 8), Is In Spawn Room(Event Player)) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, pos_cache, True, Random Value In Array(Remove From Array(Global.cowboy_tp_array, (Event Player).pos_cache)));
        Call Subroutine(cowboy_tp);
    }
}

rule ("cowboy tp subr") {
    event {
        Subroutine;
        cowboy_tp;
    }
    actions {
        While((Event Player).has_status);
            Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        While((Event Player).took_knockback);
            Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        While((Event Player).tping);
            Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, tping, True);
        Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 2));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, trail_cache, World Vector Of(Up, Event Player, Rotation And Translation));
        Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
        Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, pos_cache, False, Value In Array((Event Player).pos_cache, True));
        Teleport(Event Player, First Of((Event Player).pos_cache));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, trail, 1);
        Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, trail, False, 2, Destination and Rate);
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Abort If(Is Dead(Event Player));
        Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, Multiply(Direction Towards(Event Player, First Of((Event Player).pos_cache)), If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, First Of((Event Player).pos_cache)), >, True), 1, (Event Player).strafe)), 1, To World, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Cassidy Flashbang Explosion Effect, Team 1, Event Player, 1);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Cassidy Flashbang Explosion Sound, Team 1, Eye Position(Event Player), 200);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, tping, False);
    }
}

rule ("cowboy special attack") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Cassidy;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 14;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(Random Real(5, 7), Ignore Condition);
        Wait Until(Not((Event Player).tping), 1);
        If(And(Not((Event Player).boss_phase), Compare(Normalized Health(Event Player), <, 0.5)));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, attack, 3);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_phase, True);
        Else;
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, attack, Random Integer(True, If-Then-Else((Event Player).boss_phase, 3, 2)));
        End;
        Wait Until(Not((Event Player).attack), 15);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

        Ongoing - Each Player;

        Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }

        Modify Global Variable(summoner_effects, Append To Array, Last Text ID);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 2, 6);

            Modify Global Variable(summoner_effects, Append To Array, Last Text ID);

        End;

    event {
        Subroutine;
        boss_zoomin;
    }
    actions {

        Start Camera(Event Player, (Event Player).cutscene_cam_pos, (Event Player).cutscene_cam_lookat, 50);
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, cutscene_cam_pos, World Vector Of(Value In Array(Array(Vector(False, 1.5, 3), Vector(False, -1, 3), Vector(False, False, 3.5), Vector(False, -1, 3), Vector(False, 0.5, 3)), (Global.boss).boss_ID), Global.boss, Rotation And Translation), (Event Player).cutscene_cam_speedup, Destination and Rate);
        Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, cutscene_cam_lookat, Eye Position(Global.boss), (Event Player).cutscene_cam_speedup, Destination and Rate);
        Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, cutscene_cam_speedup, 150, 150, Destination and Rate);
    }
}

rule ("zomnic explode") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        Zenyatta;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).zomnic == 1;
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
    }
    actions {
        While(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, Global.door), >, 2));
            Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, exploding, Null);
        Stop Facing(Event Player);
        Set Status(Event Player, Null, Rooted, 9999);
        Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, exploding, 6, 6, Destination and Rate);
        Start Scaling Player(Event Player, Add(True, Multiply((Event Player).exploding, 0.1)), True);
        Create Effect(If-Then-Else(Modulo(Round To Integer((Event Player).exploding, Up), 2), All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Echo Cloning Effect, Team 1, Event Player, True, Visible To Position and Radius);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, trail, Last Created Entity);
        Wait(True, Abort When False);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Junkrat RIP Tire Explosion Effect, Team 2, Add(Position Of(Event Player), Up), 1.5);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Sigma Accretion Impact Effect, Team 1, Add(Position Of(Event Player), Up), 1.5);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Junkrat RIP Tire Explosion Sound, Team 1, Eye Position(Event Player), 200);
        Modify Global Variable(door_health, Subtract, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, -1), 10, 5));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, grillager_victims, Filtered Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 5, Team 1, Surfaces), (Current Array Element).enemy_ID));
        For Player Variable(Event Player, i, 0, Count Of((Event Player).grillager_victims), True);
            Damage(Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i)), Event Player, Multiply(40, Subtract(6, Distance Between(Event Player, Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i))))));
            Apply Impulse(Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i)), Add(Direction Towards(Event Player, Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i))), Vector(0, 0.7, 0)), 20, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
            Set Player Variable(Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i)), took_knockback, 1);
            Chase Player Variable At Rate(Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i)), took_knockback, False, True, Destination and Rate);
        End;
        Wait(0.03, Ignore Condition);
        Teleport(Event Player, Global.compressBakeMatcher);
    }
}

rule ("phase 18/20 spawning event") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Array Contains(Array(18, 20), Global.phase) == True;
    }
    actions {
        While(Not(Number Of Dead Players(Team 1)));
            Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Wait(Random Real(0.5, 1.5), Ignore Condition);
        If(And(Array Contains(Array(18, 20), Global.phase), Number Of Dead Players(Team 1)));
            Set Global Variable(enemy_ID_sequence, Array(If-Then-Else(Compare(Random Real(0, 100), <, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 7, -1)), 10, Random Value In Array(Append To Array(If-Then-Else(Compare(Random Real(0, 100), <, 35), 5, Random Integer(True, 7)), If-Then-Else(Compare(Count Of(Filtered Array(Players On Hero(Hero(Brigitte), Team 1), Is Alive(Current Array Element))), >=, 2), Empty Array, If-Then-Else(Compare(Random Real(0, 100), <, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 20, -1)), 26, Random Integer(21, 24))))))));
            Call Subroutine(spawn_enemies);
        End;
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }

    }
}

rule ("zomnic dead") {
    event {
        Player Died;
        Team 2;
        Zenyatta;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, start_pathfind, False);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Sigma Accretion Impact Effect, Team 2, World Vector Of(Up, Event Player, Rotation And Translation), 1);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Junkrat Concussion Mine Explosion Sound, Team 2, Eye Position(Event Player), 200);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Wrecking Ball Piledriver Impact Effect, Team 2, World Vector Of(Up, Event Player, Rotation And Translation), 1);
        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        If(Compare((Event Player).zomnic, ==, 2));
            Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 2, Slot Of(Event Player));
        Else;
            Teleport(Event Player, Global.compressBakeMatcher);
            Wait(Random Real(4, 6), Ignore Condition);
            Wait Until(Compare(Global.phase, !=, 19), 99999);
            If(Compare(Global.phase, ==, 21));
                Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 2, Slot Of(Event Player));
            Else If((Event Player).zomnic);
                Abort If(Is Alive(Event Player));
                Resurrect(Event Player);
                Teleport(Event Player, Random Value In Array(Global.zomnic_spawns));
                Clear Status(Event Player, Rooted);
                Stop Scaling Player(Event Player);
                Destroy Effect((Event Player).trail);
                Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, exploding);
    }
}

        Set Global Variable(dialogue_priority, False);

    }
}

rule ("zomnic path correct") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        Zenyatta;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).zomnic_top == True;
    }
    actions {
        While(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).zomnic_dest), >, 2));
            Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, zomnic_dest, Global.door);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, zomnic_top, False);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, start_pathfind, False);
        Wait(Multiply(Global.wait, 3), Ignore Condition);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, start_pathfind, True);
    }
}

rule ("zomnic stuck too long") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        Zenyatta;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).zomnic == 1;
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
        Throttle Of(Event Player) != Vector(False, False, False);
        Speed Of In Direction(Event Player, World Vector Of(Throttle Of(Event Player), Event Player, Rotation)) < 1;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(1.5, Abort When False);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, start_pathfind, False);
        Wait(Multiply(Global.wait, 3), Ignore Condition);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, start_pathfind, True);
    }
}

    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }

        Array Contains(Array(18, 20), Global.phase) == True;

        Set Global Variable(dialogue_priority, 2);
        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, True);
        Wait Until(Not(Global.main_dialogue), 99999);
        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, False);
        Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Symmetra), Custom String("This‚Ä¶ is the end for me‚Ä¶ My apologies, comrades."), 1.5)));
        Call Subroutine(main_dialogue);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 2, 7);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 2, 8);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 2, 9);
        Set Global Variable(dialogue_priority, False);
        Destroy All Progress Bar HUD Text;
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, 7);
        Start Forcing Player To Be Hero(Global.dialogue_bot, Hero(Symmetra));
        While(Compare(Global.summoner_effects, !=, Empty Array));
            Destroy Effect(First Of(Global.summoner_effects));
            Destroy In-World Text(First Of(Global.summoner_effects));

        End;

        Create Dummy Bot(Hero(Symmetra), Team 2, 6, Global.pentagram_pos, Vector(0.24, False, 0.97));
        Set Player Variable(Last Created Entity, dead_summoner, True);
    }
}

rule ("ana init") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Ana;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 20;
        (Event Player).boss_ID == 3;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, ana_target_friends, True);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, avoid_enviro, True);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, pre_init, False);
        Set Projectile Gravity(Event Player, 30);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_dealt, Add(30, Multiply(10, Global.difficulty)));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_received, Subtract(130, Multiply(15, Global.difficulty)));
        Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_dealt);
        Set Damage Received(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_received);
        Clear Status(Event Player, Phased Out);
        Set Status(Event Player, Null, Invincible, 9999);
        Start Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire));
        Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Cloud, Color(Violet), (Event Player).gas_pos, (Event Player).gas_radius, Position and Radius);
        Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring, Color(Violet), (Event Player).gas_pos, (Event Player).gas_radius, Position and Radius);
        Start Forcing Player Position(Event Player, Vector(89.137, 20, -63.627), False);
        Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).attack, >, False), Ray Cast Hit Position(Eye Position((Event Player).target), Add(Eye Position((Event Player).target), Vector(0, -10, 0)), Null, Null, True), Eye Position((Event Player).target))), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
    }
}

rule ("player poisoned") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 20;
        (Global.boss).gas_radius > False;
        Has Status(Event Player, Phased Out) == False;

            Set Player Variable(Event Player, poisoned, 5);
        End;
        Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("poison damage") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).poisoned > False;
    }
    actions {
        Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, poisoned, False, True, None);
        Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Aura, Color(Violet), Event Player, True, Position and Radius);
        Modify Player Variable(Event Player, poison_effect, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
        Create Effect(Event Player, Widowmaker Venom Mine Target Effect, Team 2, Event Player, True, Position and Radius);
        Modify Player Variable(Event Player, poison_effect, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
        While((Event Player).poisoned);
            Damage(Event Player, Global.boss, Add(2, Multiply(Global.difficulty, 1.25)));
            Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        While(Compare((Event Player).poison_effect, !=, Empty Array));
            Destroy Effect(First Of((Event Player).poison_effect));
            Modify Player Variable(Event Player, poison_effect, Remove From Array By Index, False);
        End;
    }
}

    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;

    conditions {

            Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Sigma Gravitic Flux Target Effect, Team 1, Event Player, True, Position and Radius);
        Else;
            Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ana Sleeping Effect, Team 2, Event Player, True, Position and Radius);
        End;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, speed_effect, Last Created Entity);
        Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, speed_boosted, False, True, Destination and Rate);
        Set Move Speed(Event Player, If-Then-Else(Compare(Team Of(Event Player), ==, Team 1), Multiply((Event Player).speed, 1.5), Multiply((Event Player).speed, 0.5)));
        Wait Until(Not((Event Player).speed_boosted), 99999);
        Set Move Speed(Event Player, (Event Player).speed);
        Destroy Effect((Event Player).speed_effect);
        Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, speed_boosted);
    }
}

        Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, blind_radius);
    }
