rule ("zomnic init") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        Zenyatta;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).zomnic == 1;
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Start Facing(Event Player, World Vector Of(Throttle Of(Event Player), Event Player, Rotation), 100, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        If(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, First Of(Global.zomnic_spawns)), <, 4));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, zomnic_top, True);
        Else;
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, zomnic_top, False);
        End;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, zomnic_dest, If-Then-Else((Event Player).zomnic_top, Vector(67.27, 12.72, -70.64), Global.door));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, throttle_mag, True);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, start_pathfind, True);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location, Add(Global.pentagram_pos, Vector(0, 20, 0)));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location_2, Position Of(Event Player));
        Chase Player Variable Over Time(Event Player, boss_target_location, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 1.3, None);
        Create Beam Effect(All Players(All Teams), Winston Tesla Cannon Beam, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, (Event Player).boss_target_location, Team 1, Visible To Position and Radius);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, trail_cache, Last Created Entity);
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Doomfist Meteor Strike Impact Sound, Team 1, Position Of(Event Player), 200);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Pickup Effect, Color(Orange), Event Player, 1);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion, Color(Red), Event Player, 8);
        Modify Global Variable(summoner_power, Subtract, 1.5);
        Wait(1.3, Ignore Condition);
        Destroy Effect((Event Player).trail_cache);
    }
}

rule ("phase 11 spawn subr") {
    event {
        Subroutine;
        phase_11_spawn;
    }
    actions {
        Abort If(And(Compare(Global.dragon_blood_qty, ==, 4), Compare(Global.mercy_drop, ==, 1)));
        Wait Until(Compare(Number Of Living Players(Team 1), <=, 3), 99999);
        Set Global Variable(enemy_spawn, Filtered Array(Global.enemy_spawn_2, And(Compare(Distance Between(Current Array Element, Global.last_collected_blood), <, 40), Not(Is In Line of Sight(Current Array Element, Eye Position(Global.last_collected_blood), Barriers Do Not Block LOS)))));
        If(Compare(Global.enemy_spawn, ==, Empty Array));
            Set Global Variable(enemy_spawn, Filtered Array(Global.enemy_spawn_2, Compare(Distance Between(Current Array Element, Global.last_collected_blood), <, 60)));
        End;
        If(Compare(Global.dragon_blood_qty, >, 3));
            Set Global Variable(enemy_ID_sequence, Append To Array(Array(Random Integer(True, 4), Random Integer(6, 7), Random Integer(True, 4), Random Integer(21, 23)), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 7, Empty Array)));
        Else If(Compare(Global.dragon_blood_qty, >, True));
            Set Global Variable(enemy_ID_sequence, Append To Array(Array(Random Integer(True, 4), Random Integer(True, 4), Random Integer(True, 4), Random Integer(21, 23), Random Integer(6, 7)), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.dragon_blood_qty, >, 2), 10, 7), Empty Array)));
        Else If(Compare(Global.dragon_blood_qty, >, False));
            Set Global Variable(enemy_ID_sequence, Array(Random Integer(True, 4), Random Integer(True, 4), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 10, Random Integer(True, 4)), Random Integer(21, 23), Random Integer(6, 7), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 26, Random Integer(21, 23))));
        Else;
            Set Global Variable(enemy_ID_sequence, Array(Random Integer(True, 4), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 7, Random Integer(True, 4)), Random Integer(6, 7), Random Integer(21, 23), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 26, Random Integer(21, 23)), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 9, 8)));
        End;
        Call Subroutine(spawn_enemies);
    }
}

rule ("ana nana") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Ana;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).boss_ID == 3;
        Global.ana_start_nana == True;
        Is Using Ultimate(Event Player) == False;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(Random Real(6, 8), Ignore Condition);
        Wait Until(Not((Event Player).attack), 99999);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, attack, 5);
        While(Not(Is Using Ultimate(Event Player)));
            Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, 100);
            Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ultimate));
            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location, Eye Position(Event Player));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location_2, Vector(84.326, 12.76, -81.319));
        Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, boss_target_location, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 20, Destination and Rate);
        Create Beam Effect(All Players(All Teams), Zarya Particle Beam, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, (Event Player).boss_target_location, Team 1, Visible To Position and Radius);
        Modify Player Variable(Event Player, boss_effects, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion, Color(Orange), (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 20);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion, Color(Orange), (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 35);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion, Color(Orange), (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 50);
        For Player Variable(Event Player, i2, 1, 5, 1);
            Set Player Variable(Players In Slot((Event Player).i2, Team 1), nano, 8);
            Heal(Players In Slot((Event Player).i2, Team 1), Global.boss, 200);
            Wait(0.3, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Wait Until(Compare((Event Player).boss_target_location, ==, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2), 99999);
        While(Compare((Event Player).boss_effects, !=, Empty Array));
            Destroy Effect(First Of((Event Player).boss_effects));
            Modify Player Variable(Event Player, boss_effects, Remove From Array By Index, False);
        End;
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, attack, False);
    }
}

rule ("enter castle") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 22;
        Y Component Of(Global.objective_pos) < 100;
        Is True For All(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element))), Compare(Distance Between(Current Array Element, Global.objective_pos), <, 4)) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Teleport(Remove From Array(All Players(Team 2), Global.merchant), Vector(89.583, 13.378, -61.666));
        Set Global Variable(boundary_corners_2, Array(Last Of(Global.boundary_corners), First Of(Global.boundary_corners)));
        Set Global Variable(boundary_line_2, Vector Towards(First Of(Global.boundary_corners_2), Last Of(Global.boundary_corners_2)));
        Start Rule(delete_bound_effects, Restart Rule);
        Set Global Variable(phase, 23);
        Set Global Variable(objective_pos, Global._extendedGlobalCollection);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, Slot Of((Global.merchant).attack));
        Set Global Variable(shop_open, False);
        Wait(0.4, Ignore Condition);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 2, 5);
        For Global Variable(i4, 0, 4, True);
            Set Global Variable(enemy_spawn, Value In Array(Array(Vector(94.924, 11.112, -29.514), Vector(90.221, 16.257, -21.267), Vector(106.134, 11.113, -33.421), Vector(100.805, 12.688, -46.994)), Global.i4));
            Create Dummy Bot(Hero(Brigitte), Team 1, Add(Global.i4, True), Global.enemy_spawn, Up);
            Set Player Variable(Last Created Entity, enemy_ID, Value In Array(Array(21, 22, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3), 25, 22), 25), Global.i4));
            Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
        End;
    }
}

rule ("rein double earthshatter") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Reinhardt;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).boss_ID == 4.1;
        (Global.boss).attack == 5;
    }

        For Player Variable(Event Player, i, 0, 3, 0.1);

rule ("bot stuck too long tp") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).enemy_ID > False;
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(60, Abort When False);
        If(Is Alive((Event Player).target));
            If(Not(((Event Player).target).zomnic));
                If(Not(Is In Line of Sight(Event Player, (Event Player).target, Barriers Do Not Block LOS)));
                    Teleport(Event Player, Nearest Walkable Position(World Vector Of(Vector(0, 0, -10), (Event Player).target, Rotation And Translation)));
                End;
            End;
        End;
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).enemy_ID >= True;
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
        (Event Player).safeguard_fix == False;
    }
    actions {
        Start Forcing Player To Be Hero(Event Player, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, <, 20), Hero(Torbj√∂rn), Hero(Brigitte)));
        Stop Facing(Event Player);
        Stop Scaling Barriers(Event Player);
        Stop Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire));
        Stop Scaling Player(Event Player);
        Set Knockback Received(Event Player, 100);
        Stop Modifying Hero Voice Lines(Event Player);
        Set Projectile Gravity(Event Player, 100);
        Set Projectile Speed(Event Player, 100);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, grillager_activate, False);
        Press Button(Event Player, Button(Interact));
        If(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Torbj√∂rn)));
            Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Value In Array(Array(Custom String("Villager"), Custom String("Killager"), Custom String("Skillager"), Custom String("Grillager"), Custom String("Spillager"), Custom String("Chillager"), Custom String("Instakillager"), Custom String("Overkillager"), Custom String("Overoverkillager"), Custom String("Chernobyllager")), Subtract((Event Player).enemy_ID, True)));

            Set Knockback Dealt(Event Player, 100);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, speed, 80);
            Set Move Speed(Event Player, 80);

            Set Weapon(Event Player, If-Then-Else(Array Contains(Array(1, 4, 6, 7), (Event Player).enemy_ID), 2, 1));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_dealt, Add(25, Multiply(15, Global.difficulty)));
            If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 2));
                Start Facing(Event Player, Add(Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Add(Eye Position((Event Player).target), Vector(0, -0.5, 0))), Vector(Random Real(-0.1, 0.1), False, Random Real(-0.1, 0.1))), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);

                Set Move Speed(Event Player, 60);

            Else If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 5));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_dealt, Add(10, Multiply(8, Global.difficulty)));
                Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Position Of((Event Player).target)), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                Set Projectile Gravity(Event Player, 5);
                Set Max Health(Event Player, 200);
                Set Player Health(Event Player, 99999);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 6));
                Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Mei Frozen Effect, Team 1, Event Player, True, Visible To Position and Radius);
                Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, trail, False, Last Created Entity);
                Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Mei Frozen Sound, Team 1, Event Player, 200, Visible To Position and Radius);
                Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, trail, 2, Last Created Entity);
                Set Max Health(Event Player, 150);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 7));
                Create In-World Text(All Players(All Teams), Custom String(":D"), Event Player, 2, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To Position and String, Color(Red), Default Visibility);
                Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, trail, True, Last Text ID);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_dealt, Add(300, Multiply(100, Global.difficulty)));
                Start Scaling Player(Event Player, 0.7, False);
                Set Max Health(Event Player, 37.5);

                Start Modifying Hero Voice Lines(Event Player, 0.75, True);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 9));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, speed, 70);
                Set Move Speed(Event Player, 70);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_dealt, Add(40, Multiply(15, Global.difficulty)));
                Start Scaling Player(Event Player, 2.2, False);
                Set Max Health(Event Player, Absolute Value(3000));
                Set Knockback Received(Event Player, 30);
                Set Player Health(Event Player, 99999);
                Start Modifying Hero Voice Lines(Event Player, 0.5, True);

                Set Player Variable(Event Player, speed, 70);
                Set Move Speed(Event Player, 70);

            End;
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_received, Subtract(130, Multiply(15, Global.difficulty)));
            Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_dealt);
            Set Damage Received(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_received);
        Else If(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Brigitte)));
            Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Value In Array(Array(Custom String("Guard"), Custom String("Vanguard"), Custom String("Lifeguard"), Custom String("Safeguard"), Custom String("Royal Guard"), Custom String("Bitter Guard")), Subtract((Event Player).enemy_ID, 21)));
            Set Projectile Speed(Event Player, 60);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, speed, 80);
            Set Move Speed(Event Player, 80);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_dealt, Add(25, Multiply(10, Global.difficulty)));
            Set Max Health(Event Player, 41.667);
            Set Knockback Dealt(Event Player, 140);
            Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire), False);
            Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Event Player).target)), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_received, Subtract(130, Multiply(15, Global.difficulty)));
            Set Damage Received(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_received);
            If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 23));
                Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Heal Target Active Effect, Team 1, Event Player, True, Visible To Position and Radius);
                Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, trail, False, Last Created Entity);
                Create In-World Text(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("+"), Event Player, 2, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To Position and String, Color(Yellow), Default Visibility);
                Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, trail, True, Last Text ID);
                Set Healing Dealt(Event Player, 100);
            Else;
                Set Healing Dealt(Event Player, 0);
            End;
            If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 24));
                Start Scaling Barriers(Event Player, 5, True);
                Start Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire));
                Set Max Health(Event Player, 27.778);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_dealt, Add(50, Multiply(25, Global.difficulty)));
            End;
            If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 25));
                Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Wrecking Ball Adaptive Shield Target Effect, Team 1, Event Player, True, Visible To Position and Radius);
                Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, trail, False, Last Created Entity);
                Create In-World Text(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("Œ©"), Event Player, 2, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To Position and String, Color(Orange), Default Visibility);
                Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, trail, True, Last Text ID);
                Set Max Health(Event Player, 55.556);
                Set Move Speed(Event Player, 69);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_dealt, Add(37.5, Multiply(15, Global.difficulty)));
            End;
            If(Compare((Event Player).enemy_ID, ==, 26));
                Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Good Aura, Color(Purple), Event Player, True, Visible To Position and Radius);
                Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, trail, False, Last Created Entity);
                Create In-World Text(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("‚Äì"), Event Player, 2, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To Position and String, Color(Purple), Default Visibility);
                Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, trail, True, Last Text ID);
                Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring, Color(Purple), Event Player, 8, Visible To Position and Radius);
                Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, trail, 2, Last Created Entity);
                Set Max Health(Event Player, 55.556);
            End;
            Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_dealt);
    }
}

rule ("rein init") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Reinhardt;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 26;
        (Event Player).boss_ID == 4;
    }
    actions {
        Create Progress Bar In-World Text(All Players(All Teams), Multiply(Normalized Health(Event Player), 100), Custom String("The Lord Of Adlersbrunn"), Event Player, 0.5, Clip Against Surfaces, Color(Red), Color(Red), Visible To Position and Values, Default Visibility);
        Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, effects, False, Last Text ID);
        Set Move Speed(Event Player, 150);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, speed, 80);
        Set Move Speed(Event Player, 80);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, rein_throttle_mag, 1);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, pre_init, False);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, turn_rate, 1000);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_dealt, Add(60, Multiply(20, Global.difficulty)));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_received, Subtract(130, Multiply(15, Global.difficulty)));
        Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_dealt);
        Set Damage Received(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_received);
        Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Event Player).target)), (Event Player).turn_rate, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        Clear Status(Event Player, Phased Out);
        Destroy Effect((Event Player).immune_effect);
        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        Abort If(Compare(Global.dialogue_priority, >=, 3));
        Set Global Variable(dialogue_priority, 2);
        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, True);
        Wait Until(Not(Global.main_dialogue), 99999);
        Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, False);
        Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("Despite The Doctor‚Äôs taunting, the old Lord‚Äôs spirit did not falter."), 1), Array(Hero(Reinhardt), Custom String("He mustered every ounce of his courage, such that he would never be shaken by his terrifying adversaries!"), 1.5)));
        Call Subroutine(main_dialogue);
        Set Global Variable(dialogue_priority, False);
        Set Status(Event Player, Null, Phased Out, 9999);
        Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), L√∫cio Sound Barrier Protected Effect, Team 1, Event Player, True, Visible To Position and Radius);
        Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, effects, True, Last Created Entity);
        Create Dummy Bot(Hero(Reinhardt), Team 1, 6, Position Of(Event Player), Facing Direction Of(Event Player));
        Set Player Variable(Last Created Entity, boss_ID, 4.1);
        Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, boss_pet, False, Last Created Entity);
        Small Message(All Players(Team 2), Custom String("The Lord is now immune to stuns and knockback."));
    }

rule ("dont get stuck on chandelier") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Reinhardt;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).boss_ID == 4;
        Y Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)) > 18;
        Is On Ground(Event Player) == True;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare(Distance Between(Vector(118.855, 18.777, -44.782), Event Player), <, 4));
            Disable Movement Collision With Environment(Event Player, True);
            Wait Until(Compare(Distance Between(Vector(118.855, 18.777, -44.782), Event Player), >, 4.5), 99999);
            Enable Movement Collision With Environment(Event Player);
        End;
        Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Reinhardt;
    }

        Global.phase == 26;

        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, 6);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, 7);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, 8);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, 9);
        Clear Status(Event Player, Phased Out);
        Stop Facing(Event Player);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, nano, Null);
        Destroy All Progress Bar In-World Text;
        While(Compare((Event Player).effects, !=, Empty Array));
            Destroy Effect(First Of((Event Player).effects));
            Modify Player Variable(Event Player, effects, Remove From Array By Index, False);
        End;
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, True);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, 2);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, 3);
        Destroy Dummy Bot(Team 1, 4);
        Kill(Event Player, Null);
        Set Global Variable(last_player_to_die, Event Player);
    }

    }

rule ("boss special attack followup") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).attack > False;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 1));
            If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 1));
                Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, Multiply((Event Player).damage_dealt, 2));
                Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
                Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
                Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_dealt);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 2));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, no_jump, True);
                Respawn(Value In Array((Event Player).boss_pet, True));
                Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
                Wait Until(Is On Ground(Event Player), 5);
                Stop Facing(Event Player);
                Set Move Speed(Event Player, False);
                Start Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Crouch));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location, Ray Cast Hit Position(Eye Position(Event Player), Add(Eye Position(Event Player), Multiply(Facing Direction Of(Event Player), 8)), Null, Event Player, True));
                Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
                Wait Until(Not((Event Player).has_status), 10);
                Stop Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Crouch));
                Set Status(Event Player, Null, Phased Out, True);
                For Player Variable(Event Player, i, 0, 2, True);
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Widowmaker Venom Mine Explosion Effect, Team 1, World Vector Of(Up, Event Player, Rotation And Translation), 1);
                    Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location_2, Ray Cast Hit Position((Event Player).boss_target_location, Add((Event Player).boss_target_location, Multiply(Direction From Angles(Random Real(0, 360), 0), 7.5)), Null, Event Player, True));
                    Teleport(Event Player, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2);
                    Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                    Set Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards((Event Player).boss_target_location_2, (Event Player).boss_target_location), To World);
                    While(Not(Is Using Ability 1(Event Player)));
                        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                        Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
                    End;
                    If(Compare((Event Player).i, <, 2));
                        Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
                        Start Rule(genji_pet_strike, Restart Rule);
                    End;
                    Wait Until(Not(Is Using Ability 1(Event Player)), 1);
                End;
                Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
                Set Invisible(Value In Array((Event Player).boss_pet, True), All);
                Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Event Player).target)), (Event Player).turn_rate, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                Set Move Speed(Event Player, 70);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, no_jump, False);
                Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Widowmaker Venom Mine Explosion Effect, Team 1, World Vector Of(Up, Value In Array((Event Player).boss_pet, True), Rotation And Translation), 1);
                Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                Teleport(Value In Array((Event Player).boss_pet, True), Global._extendedGlobalCollection);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 3));
                For Player Variable(Event Player, i, 0, 3, True);
                    Cancel Primary Action(First Of((Event Player).boss_pet));
                    Set Ability Cooldown(First Of((Event Player).boss_pet), Button(Ability 2), False);
                    Press Button(First Of((Event Player).boss_pet), Button(Ability 2));
                    Wait(0.2, Abort When False);
                    Press Button(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire));
                    Wait(0.8, Abort When False);
                End;
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, attack, False);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 4));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, no_jump, True);
                Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
                Wait Until(Is On Ground(Event Player), 5);
                Apply Impulse(Event Player, Up, 10, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
                Wait(0.5, Ignore Condition);
                Press Button(Event Player, Button(Jump));
                Apply Impulse(Event Player, World Vector Of(Vector(False, True, -3), Event Player, Rotation), 15, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
                Wait(0.05, Abort When False);
                Set Status(Event Player, Null, Frozen, 2);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, attack, 4.1);
                Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, attack, 4.2);
                Wait(2, Ignore Condition);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, no_jump, False);
            End;
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 2));
            If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 1));
                Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, pos_cache, True, Nearest Walkable Position(Ray Cast Hit Position(Eye Position((Event Player).target), Add(Eye Position((Event Player).target), Multiply(Direction From Angles(Random Real(0, 360), 0), 10)), Null, Event Player, True)));
                Call Subroutine(cowboy_tp);
                Wait(0.7, Ignore Condition);
                While(Not(Is Firing Secondary(Event Player)));
                    Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                    Press Button(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire));
                End;
                Wait(2, Ignore Condition);
                Cancel Primary Action(Event Player);
                Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, pos_cache, True, Random Value In Array(Remove From Array(Global.cowboy_tp_array, (Event Player).pos_cache)));
                Call Subroutine(cowboy_tp);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 2));
                Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
                For Player Variable(Event Player, i, 0, Random Integer(3, 5), True);
                    Press Button((Event Player).boss_pet, Button(Ability 2));
                    Wait(0.7, Ignore Condition);
                End;
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 3));
                Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Event Player).target)), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, Multiply((Event Player).damage_dealt, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, <=, 0), 0.6, 1)));
                For Player Variable(Event Player, i, 0, Random Integer(True, 3), True);
                    If(Is True For Any(Global.cowboy_tp_array, Is In Line of Sight(Add(Current Array Element, Up), Eye Position((Event Player).target), Barriers Do Not Block LOS)));
                        Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, pos_cache, True, Random Value In Array(Remove From Array(Filtered Array(Global.cowboy_tp_array, Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position((Event Player).target), Add(Current Array Element, Up), Barriers Do Not Block LOS)), (Event Player).pos_cache)));
                    Else;
                        Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, pos_cache, True, Nearest Walkable Position(Ray Cast Hit Position(Eye Position((Event Player).target), Add(Eye Position((Event Player).target), Multiply(Direction From Angles(Random Real(0, 360), 0), 10)), Null, Event Player, True)));
                    End;
                    Call Subroutine(cowboy_tp);
                    Stop Throttle In Direction(Event Player);
                    While(Not(Is Using Ultimate(Event Player)));
                        Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, 100);
                        Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ultimate));
                        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                    End;
                    Wait(Random Real(2.5, 3), Ignore Condition);
                    Press Button(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire));
                    Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                    Press Button(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire));
                    Wait Until(Not(Is Using Ultimate(Event Player)), 2);
                End;
                Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, (Event Player).damage_dealt);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, attack, False);
                Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Add(Add(Eye Position((Event Player).target), Vector(0, -0.5, 0)), Vector(Random Real(-0.8, 0.8), False, Random Real(-0.8, 0.8)))), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, pos_cache, True, Random Value In Array(Remove From Array(Global.cowboy_tp_array, (Event Player).pos_cache)));
                Call Subroutine(cowboy_tp);
            End;
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 3));
            If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 1));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, ana_target_friends, False);
                Wait(0.5, Ignore Condition);
                Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
                Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
                Cancel Primary Action(Event Player);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location, Eye Position(Event Player));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location_2, Ray Cast Hit Position(Eye Position(Event Player), Add(Eye Position(Event Player), Multiply(Facing Direction Of(Event Player), 100)), Null, Null, True));
                Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, boss_target_location, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 40, Destination and Rate);
                Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Orb, Color(Violet), Update Every Frame((Event Player).boss_target_location), 0.2, Position and Radius);
                Modify Player Variable(Event Player, boss_effects, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
                Create Beam Effect(All Players(All Teams), Zarya Particle Beam, Update Every Frame((Event Player).boss_target_location), Add((Event Player).boss_target_location, Multiply(Direction Towards((Event Player).boss_target_location_2, Eye Position(Event Player)), 2)), Team 2, Visible To Position and Radius);
                Modify Player Variable(Event Player, boss_effects, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
                Wait Until(Compare((Event Player).boss_target_location, ==, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2), 99999);
                While(Compare((Event Player).boss_effects, !=, Empty Array));
                    Destroy Effect(First Of((Event Player).boss_effects));
                    Modify Player Variable(Event Player, boss_effects, Remove From Array By Index, False);
                End;
                Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Explosion, Color(Violet), (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 5);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, gas_pos, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, gas_radius, Null);
                Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, gas_radius, 6, 4, Destination and Rate);
                Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ana Biotic Grenade Explosion Sound, Team 1, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 200);
                Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ana Biotic Grenade Explosion Effect, Team 1, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 1);
                Damage(Players Within Radius((Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 4, Team 2, Surfaces), Event Player, 60);
                Heal(Players Within Radius((Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 4, Team 1, Surfaces), Event Player, 100);
                Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, ana_target_friends, True);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 2));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, ana_target_friends, False);
                Wait(0.5, Ignore Condition);
                Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 2));
                Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, ana_target_friends, True);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 3));
                Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
                Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
                Cancel Primary Action(Event Player);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location, Eye Position(Event Player));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location_2, Ray Cast Hit Position(Eye Position(Event Player), Add(Eye Position(Event Player), Multiply(Facing Direction Of(Event Player), 100)), Null, Null, True));
                Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, boss_target_location, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 40, Destination and Rate);
                Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Orb, Color(Aqua), Update Every Frame((Event Player).boss_target_location), 0.2, Position and Radius);
                Modify Player Variable(Event Player, boss_effects, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
                Create Beam Effect(All Players(All Teams), Echo Focusing Beam, Update Every Frame((Event Player).boss_target_location), Add((Event Player).boss_target_location, Multiply(Direction Towards((Event Player).boss_target_location_2, Eye Position(Event Player)), 2)), Team 2, Visible To Position and Radius);
                Modify Player Variable(Event Player, boss_effects, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
                Wait Until(Compare((Event Player).boss_target_location, ==, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2), 99999);
                While(Compare((Event Player).boss_effects, !=, Empty Array));
                    Destroy Effect(First Of((Event Player).boss_effects));
                    Modify Player Variable(Event Player, boss_effects, Remove From Array By Index, False);
                End;
                Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Explosion, Color(Aqua), (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 5);
                Set Player Variable(Players Within Radius((Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 5, Team 1, Off), speed_boosted, 8);
                Set Player Variable(Players Within Radius((Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 5, Team 2, Off), speed_boosted, 4);
                Damage(Players Within Radius((Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 4, Team 2, Surfaces), Event Player, 60);
                Heal(Players Within Radius((Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 4, Team 1, Surfaces), Event Player, 100);
                Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
                Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ana Biotic Grenade Explosion Sound, Team 1, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 200);
                Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ana Biotic Grenade Explosion Effect, Team 1, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 1);
                Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 4));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, ana_target_friends, False);
                Wait(0.5, Ignore Condition);
                Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
                Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
                Cancel Primary Action(Event Player);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location, Eye Position(Event Player));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location_2, Ray Cast Hit Position(Eye Position(Event Player), Add(Eye Position(Event Player), Multiply(Facing Direction Of(Event Player), 100)), Null, Null, True));
                Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, boss_target_location, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 40, Destination and Rate);
                Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Orb, Color(Black), Update Every Frame((Event Player).boss_target_location), 0.2, Position and Radius);
                Modify Player Variable(Event Player, boss_effects, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
                Create Beam Effect(All Players(All Teams), Moira Coalescence Beam, Update Every Frame((Event Player).boss_target_location), Add((Event Player).boss_target_location, Multiply(Direction Towards((Event Player).boss_target_location_2, Eye Position(Event Player)), 2)), Team 2, Visible To Position and Radius);
                Modify Player Variable(Event Player, boss_effects, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
                Wait Until(Compare((Event Player).boss_target_location, ==, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2), 99999);
                While(Compare((Event Player).boss_effects, !=, Empty Array));
                    Destroy Effect(First Of((Event Player).boss_effects));
                    Modify Player Variable(Event Player, boss_effects, Remove From Array By Index, False);
                End;
                Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Explosion, Color(Black), (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 5);
                Set Player Variable(Players Within Radius((Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 5, Team 2, Surfaces), blind, 4);
                Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ana Biotic Grenade Explosion Sound, Team 1, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 200);
                Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ana Biotic Grenade Explosion Effect, Team 1, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 1);
                Damage(Players Within Radius((Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 4, Team 2, Surfaces), Event Player, 60);
                Heal(Players Within Radius((Event Player).boss_target_location_2, 4, Team 1, Surfaces), Event Player, 100);
                Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, ana_target_friends, True);
            End;
        Else If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 4));
            If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 1));
                Set Move Speed(Event Player, Multiply((Event Player).speed, 2));
                While(Not(Is Using Ability 1(Event Player)));
                    Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
                    Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                End;
                Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
                Wait Until(Not(Is Using Ability 1(Event Player)), 4);
                Set Move Speed(Event Player, (Event Player).speed);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 2));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, rein_throttle_mag, False);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, no_jump, True);
                Start Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Crouch));
                Set Projectile Speed(Event Player, 150);
                Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
                Start Facing(Event Player, Add(Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Event Player).target)), Vector(Random Real(-0.5, 0.5), False, Random Real(-0.5, 0.5))), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                For Player Variable(Event Player, i, 0, 5, True);
                    Cancel Primary Action(Event Player);
                    Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 2));
                    Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
                    Cancel Primary Action(First Of((Event Player).boss_pet));
                    Press Button(First Of((Event Player).boss_pet), Button(Ability 2));
                    Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
                    If(Has Status(Event Player, Rooted));
                        Break;
                    End;
                End;
                Stop Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Crouch));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, rein_throttle_mag, True);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, no_jump, False);
                Set Projectile Speed(Event Player, 100);
                Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Event Player).target)), (Event Player).turn_rate, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 3));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, turn_rate, False);
                Cancel Primary Action(Event Player);
                Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, 100);
                Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ultimate));
                Apply Impulse(Event Player, Up, 7, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
                Wait(0.5, Ignore Condition);
                Wait Until(Is On Ground(Event Player), 10);
                Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, turn_rate, 1000);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 4));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, rein_throttle_mag, False);
                For Player Variable(Event Player, i2, 0, 5, True);
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, turn_rate, False);
                    Set Move Speed(Event Player, Multiply(5, Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target)));
                    Set Gravity(Event Player, Max(50, Subtract(200, Multiply(5, Distance Between(Event Player, (Event Player).target)))));
                    While(Not(Is Using Ability 1(Event Player)));
                        Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
                        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                    End;
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Winston Jump Pack Landing Effect, Team 1, Position Of(Event Player), 1);
                    Apply Impulse(Event Player, Up, 20, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
                    Wait(0.5, Ignore Condition);
                    Wait Until(Is On Ground(Event Player), 10);
                    Cancel Primary Action(Event Player);
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Doomfist Meteor Strike Impact Effect, Team 1, Position Of(Event Player), 1);
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Doomfist Meteor Strike Impact Sound, Team 1, Position Of(Event Player), 200);
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, grillager_victims, Filtered Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 8, Team 2, Surfaces And Enemy Barriers), And(Is Alive(Current Array Element), Not(And(Compare(Hero Of(Current Array Element), ==, Hero(Reaper)), Is Using Ability 1(Current Array Element))))));
                    For Player Variable(Event Player, i, 0, Count Of((Event Player).grillager_victims), True);
                        Damage(Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i)), Event Player, Multiply(37.5, Subtract(9, Distance Between(Event Player, Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i))))));
                        Apply Impulse(Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i)), Direction From Angles(Horizontal Angle From Direction(Direction Towards(Event Player, Value In Array((Event Player).grillager_victims, Evaluate Once((Event Player).i)))), -37), 18, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
                    End;
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, turn_rate, 1000);
                    Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
                    If(Has Status(Event Player, Rooted));
                        Break;
                    End;
                End;
                Set Move Speed(Event Player, (Event Player).speed);
                Set Gravity(Event Player, 100);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, rein_throttle_mag, True);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).attack, ==, 5));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, rein_throttle_mag, False);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, no_jump, True);
                Start Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Crouch));
                Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
                Start Facing(Event Player, (Event Player).boss_target_location, 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                Start Facing(First Of((Event Player).boss_pet), Multiply((Event Player).boss_target_location, -1), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                For Player Variable(Event Player, i, 0, 3, 0.1);
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location, Direction From Angles(Random Real(0, 360), 0));
                    Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, 100);
                    Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
                    Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ultimate));
                    If(Has Status(Event Player, Rooted));
                        Break;
                    End;
                End;
                Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
                Stop Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Crouch));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, rein_throttle_mag, True);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, no_jump, False);
                Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Event Player).target)), (Event Player).turn_rate, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                Start Facing(First Of((Event Player).boss_pet), Facing Direction Of(Event Player), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
            End;
        End;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, attack, False);
    }
}

rule ("all player init") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        All;
    }
    actions {
        Disable Built-In Game Mode Respawning(Event Player);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, burner, Empty Array);
        Wait(0.05, Ignore Condition);
        If(Compare(Team Of(Event Player), ==, Team 1));
            If(Compare(Global.dialogue_bot, ==, Event Player));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, no_dialogue, True);
                Set Invisible(Event Player, All);
                Set Status(Event Player, Null, Phased Out, 9999);
                Set Status(Event Player, Null, Invincible, 9999);
                Set Gravity(Event Player, False);
                Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("Dialogue-chan"));
                Start Forcing Player Position(Event Player, If-Then-Else(Global.vocalisation, First Of(Filtered Array(Players On Hero(Global.main_speaker, All Teams), And(Not((Current Array Element).no_dialogue), Compare(Hero Of(Current Array Element), !=, Hero(Reinhardt))))), Vector(9999, 9999, 9999)), True);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, pre_init, True);
                Disable Movement Collision With Players(Event Player);
            Else If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, >, 0.9));
                If(Array Contains(Array(1, 2, 3, 4), (Event Player).boss_ID));
                    Set Max Health(Event Player, Multiply(Value In Array(Array(Null, 500, 500, 500, 12500), (Event Player).boss_ID), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, -1), 0.777, 1)));
                    Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Value In Array(Array(Null, Custom String("The Swordsman"), Custom String("The Gunslinger"), Custom String("The Alchemist"), Custom String("The Lord of Adlersbrunn")), (Event Player).boss_ID));
                    Set Status(Event Player, Null, Phased Out, 9999);
                    If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 1));
                        While(Not(Is Using Ability 1(Event Player)));
                            Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
                            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                        End;
                        Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
                        Set Facing(Event Player, World Vector Of(Vector(False, -1, 3), Event Player, Rotation), To World);
                        While(Not(Is Using Ultimate(Event Player)));
                            Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, 100);
                            Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ultimate));
                            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                        End;
                        Big Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("The Swordsman"));
                    Else If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 2));
                        Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, World Vector Of(Right, Event Player, Rotation), 1, To World, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
                        Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
                        While(Not(Is Using Ability 1(Event Player)));
                            Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
                            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                        End;
                        While(Not(Is Using Ultimate(Event Player)));
                            Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, 100);
                            Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ultimate));
                            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                        End;
                        Stop Throttle In Direction(Event Player);
                        Big Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("The Gunslinger"));
                    Else If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 3));
                        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ana Biotic Grenade Explosion Effect, Team 1, Position Of(Event Player), 1);
                        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ana Biotic Grenade Explosion Sound, Team 1, Position Of(Event Player), 200);
                        While(Not(Is Using Ultimate(Event Player)));
                            Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, 100);
                            Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ultimate));
                            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                        End;
                        Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ana Nano Boosted Effect, Team 1, Event Player, True, Visible To Position and Radius);
                        Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, trail, False, Last Created Entity);
                        Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ana Nano Boosted Sound, Team 1, Event Player, 200, Visible To Position and Radius);
                        Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, trail, True, Last Created Entity);
                        Big Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("The Alchemist"));
                    Else If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 4));
                        While(Not(Is Using Ability 1(Event Player)));
                            Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
                            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                        End;
                        Wait(1.2, Ignore Condition);
                        Cancel Primary Action(Event Player);
                        Set Facing(Event Player, World Vector Of(Vector(False, -0.5, 3), Event Player, Rotation), To World);
                        Big Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("The Lord Of Adlersbrunn"));
                        While(Not(Is Using Ultimate(Event Player)));
                            Set Ultimate Charge(Event Player, 100);
                            Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ultimate));
                            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                        End;
                    End;
                    Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
                    Set Player Health(Event Player, 999999);
                Else If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 5));
                    Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("Brazillager"));
                    Set Move Speed(Event Player, 200);
                    Set Max Health(Event Player, Absolute Value(2000));
                    Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, 100);
                    Set Knockback Dealt(Event Player, 300);
                    Set Damage Received(Event Player, 70);
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, pre_init, True);
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, avoid_enviro, True);
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, random, Facing Direction Of(Event Player));
                    Start Throttle In Direction(Event Player, (Event Player).random, 1, To World, Replace existing throttle, Direction and Magnitude);
                    Start Facing(Event Player, Add(Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Add(Eye Position((Event Player).target), Vector(0, -0.5, 0))), Vector(Random Real(-0.1, 0.1), False, Random Real(-0.1, 0.1))), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                    Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, real, Ultimate Charge Percent(Event Player), 1000, Destination and Rate);
                    Create Progress Bar In-World Text(All Players(All Teams), (Event Player).real, Custom String("{0} Ultimate Charge", Ability Icon String(Hero(L√∫cio), Button(Ultimate))), Event Player, 0.4, Do Not Clip, Custom Color(110, 255, 84, 255), Custom Color(110, 255, 84, 255), Visible To and Values, Default Visibility);
                    Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                    Set Player Health(Event Player, 999999);
                Else;
                    Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, (Global.boss).damage_dealt);
                    Set Status(Event Player, Null, Phased Out, 9999);
                    Set Invisible(Event Player, All);
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, pre_init, True);
                    If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 1.1));
                        Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("The Swordsman"));
                    Else If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 1.2));
                        Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("Dragon's Breath"));
                        Attach Players(Event Player, Global.boss, Vector(False, -1.15, False));
                        Start Facing(Event Player, Facing Direction Of(Global.boss), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                        Disable Movement Collision With Environment(Event Player, True);
                        Start Modifying Hero Voice Lines(Event Player, 1.2, True);
                    Else If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 1.3));
                        Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("Dragonstrike"));
                        Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Add(Eye Position((Global.boss).target), Multiply(Vector(X Component Of(Velocity Of((Global.boss).target)), False, Z Component Of(Velocity Of((Global.boss).target))), Divide(Distance Between(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Global.boss).target)), 20)))), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                        Attach Players(Event Player, Global.boss, Vector(False, False, False));
                        Disable Movement Collision With Environment(Event Player, True);
                        Start Modifying Hero Voice Lines(Event Player, 1.2, True);
                        Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, Multiply((Global.boss).damage_dealt, 1.5));
                    Else If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 2.1));
                        Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("Dynamite"));
                        Attach Players(Event Player, Global.boss, Vector(False, False, False));
                        Set Projectile Gravity(Event Player, 30);
                        Disable Movement Collision With Environment(Event Player, True);
                        Start Modifying Hero Voice Lines(Event Player, 0.6, True);
                        Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Add(Position Of((Global.boss).target), Vector(0, -0.1, 0))), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                    Else If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 4.1));
                        Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("The Lord of Adlersbrunn"));
                        Set Max Health(Event Player, Absolute Value(2500));
                        Clear Status(Event Player, Phased Out);
                        Set Status(Event Player, Null, Unkillable, 9999);
                        Attach Players(Event Player, Global.boss, Vector(False, False, False));
                        Start Facing(Event Player, Facing Direction Of(Global.boss), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                        Set Damage Received(Event Player, (Global.boss).damage_received);
                        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                        Set Player Health(Event Player, 99999);
                    Else If(Array Contains(Array(4.2, 4.3), (Event Player).boss_ID));
                        Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("Plot Armour"));
                        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Pickup Effect, Color(Red), Event Player, 2);
                        Set Invisible(Event Player, None);
                        Start Scaling Player(Event Player, False, False);
                        Start Scaling Barriers(Event Player, 7.5, False);
                        Start Forcing Player Position(Event Player, Add(Add(Position Of(Global.boss), Up), Multiply(Direction From Angles(Global.pentagram_angle, 0), If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 4.2), 3, -3))), True);
                        Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Add(Position Of(Global.boss), Up), Position Of(Event Player)), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                        Start Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire));
                    Else If(Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 4.4));
                        Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("Rammstein"));
                        Set Move Speed(Event Player, 400);
                        Set Invisible(Event Player, None);
                        Start Forcing Player Position(Event Player, World Vector Of(Vector(0.5, Add(0.5, Multiply(0.3, Sine From Degrees(Global.pentagram_angle))), -1), Global.boss, Rotation And Translation), True);
                        Start Facing(Event Player, Facing Direction Of(Global.boss), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                        Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, Multiply((Global.boss).damage_dealt, 1.5));
                        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Pickup Effect, Color(Red), Event Player, 2);
                        Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
                        Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Echo Cloning Effect, Team 1, Event Player, 5, Visible To Position and Radius);
                    End;
                End;
            End;
        Else;
            If(Is Dummy Bot(Event Player));
                If(Compare(Event Player, ==, First Of(Global.merchant)));
                    Disable Nameplates(Event Player, All Players(All Teams));
                    Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("The Merchant"));
                    Set Status(Event Player, Null, Phased Out, 9999);
                    Wait(2, Ignore Condition);
                    While(Not(Is Using Ability 1(Event Player)));
                        Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1), False);
                        Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
                        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
                    End;
                    Wait(0.4, Ignore Condition);
                    Teleport(Event Player, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.phase, ==, 7), Vector(3.272, 6.277, -70.538), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.phase, >=, 16), Vector(74.474, 11.19, -110.302), Null)));
                    Start Camera(All Players(All Teams), World Vector Of(Vector(False, 2, 4), Event Player, Rotation And Translation), Eye Position(Event Player), 0);
                    Wait Until(Not(Is Using Ability 1(Event Player)), 1);
                    Communicate(Event Player, Hello);
                    Enable Nameplates(Event Player, All Players(All Teams));
                    Wait(2, Ignore Condition);
                    Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position(First Of(Sorted Array(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Compare(Slot Of(Current Array Element), <, 4)), Distance Between(Event Player, Current Array Element))))), 500, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                    Set Global Variable(shop_open, True);
                    Stop Camera(All Players(All Teams));
                    Wait Until(Global.shop_open, 99999);
                    Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring, Color(Purple), Add(World Vector Of(Up, Event Player, Rotation And Translation), Multiply(Evaluate Once(Facing Direction Of(Event Player)), 0.2)), 3, Visible To Position and Radius);
                    Create In-World Text(Filtered Array(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 3, All Teams, Surfaces), Not(Or((Current Array Element).is_downed, (Current Array Element).shop))), Custom String("Press ''{0}'' to shop", Input Binding String(Button(Interact))), World Vector Of(Vector(0, 1.5, 0), Event Player, Rotation And Translation), 2, Do Not Clip, Visible To Position and String, Color(Purple), Default Visibility);
                    Create Dummy Bot(Hero(Moira), Team 1, -1, Add(Last Of(Global.shop_campos), Down), Direction Towards(Last Of(Global.shop_campos), First Of(Global.shop_campos)));
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, attack, Last Created Entity);
                    Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name((Event Player).attack, Custom String("The Merchant"));
                    Set Player Variable((Event Player).attack, no_dialogue, True);
                    Set Player Variable((Event Player).attack, pre_init, True);
                    Disable Nameplates((Event Player).attack, All Players(All Teams));
                    While(Not(Is Using Ability 2((Event Player).attack)));
                        Press Button((Event Player).attack, Button(Ability 2));
                        Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
                    End;
                    Start Forcing Player Outlines((Event Player).attack, All Players(All Teams), True, Color(Purple), Default);
                    Call Subroutine(shop_ui_setup);
                Else If(Compare(Event Player, ==, Global.summoner));
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, pre_init, True);
                    Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("The Summoner"));
                    Set Status(Event Player, Null, Phased Out, 9999);
                    Set Status(Event Player, Null, Burning, 9999);
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion, Color(Red), Event Player, 14);
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Pickup Effect, Color(Orange), Position Of(Event Player), 2);
                    Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Sombra EMP Explosion Sound, Color(Orange), Eye Position(Event Player), 200);
                    Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
                    Communicate(Event Player, Hello);
                    Skip If(Compare(Global.phase, >, 18), True);
                    Big Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("The Summoner"));
                    Wait(1.1, Ignore Condition);
                    Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position(First Of(Sorted Array(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Compare(Slot Of(Current Array Element), <, 4)), Distance Between(Event Player, Current Array Element))))), 500, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                Else If((Event Player).dead_summoner);
                    Set Status(Event Player, Null, Burning, 9999);
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Sombra EMP Explosion Sound, Color(Orange), Eye Position(Event Player), 200);
                    Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("The Summoner"));
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion, Color(Red), Event Player, 14);
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Pickup Effect, Color(Orange), Position Of(Event Player), 2);
                    Kill(Event Player, Null);
                    Set Status(All Players(Team 2), Null, Invincible, 9999);
                    Set Global Variable(last_player_to_die, Event Player);
                Else If(Compare((Event Player).zomnic, ==, 1));
                    Set Healing Received(Event Player, 10);
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, no_jump, True);
                    Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("Zomnic"));
                    Set Move Speed(Event Player, 35);
                    Set Max Health(Event Player, 1);
                    Add Health Pool To Player(Event Player, Health, 150, True, True);
                Else If(Compare((Event Player).zomnic, ==, 2));
                    Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("Zombardier"));
                    Set Ammo(Event Player, False, 9999);
                    Start Facing(Event Player, If-Then-Else((Event Player).target, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), World Vector Of(Up, (Event Player).target, Rotation And Translation)), Facing Direction Of(Global.junkrat)), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                    Start Scaling Player(Event Player, 1.4, False);
                    Start Forcing Player Position(Event Player, Add(Position Of(Global.junkrat), Vector(2, Add(0.3, Multiply(0.3, Sine From Degrees(Global.pentagram_angle))), 2)), True);
                    Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, 100);
                    Set Max Health(Event Player, 600);
                    Start Modifying Hero Voice Lines(Event Player, 0.75, False);
                    Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Doomfist Meteor Strike Impact Sound, Team 1, Position Of(Event Player), 200);
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Pickup Effect, Color(Orange), Event Player, 1);
                    Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring Explosion, Color(Red), Event Player, 8);
                    Set Player Health(Event Player, 99999);
                    Start Holding Button(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire));
                Else If(Compare(Event Player, ==, Global.faq_bot));
                    Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("Zommy, the FAQ Zomnic"));
                    Create In-World Text(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 3.5, All Teams, Off), Custom String("Check the WORKSHOP SETTINGS page to change the difficulty or subtitle speed!{0}(Go to ''Show Lobby'', then ''Settings'' in th{1}", Global.newline, Custom String("e top right, then ''Workshop Settings'' in the bottom left!){0}{0}{1}", Global.newline, Custom String("If the gamemode keeps crashing, try changing the ''Data Center Preference'' to ''Singapore 2''.{0}(Go to ''Show Lobby'', then{1}", Global.newline, Custom String(" ''Settings'' in the top right, then ''Lobby'' in the top middle and check under ''Match''!)")))), Event Player, True, Do Not Clip, Visible To Position and String, Custom Color(145, 227, 153, 255), Default Visibility);
                    Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
                    Teleport(Event Player, Vector(-12.94, True, -0.41));
                    Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position(First Of(Sorted Array(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Compare(Slot Of(Current Array Element), <, 4)), Distance Between(Event Player, Current Array Element))))), 500, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                End;
            Else;
                Disable Game Mode HUD(Event Player);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, scrolls_equip, Empty Array);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_received, 100);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_dealt, 100);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, speed, 100);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, scrolls_random, Randomized Array(Array(Null, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5)));
                If(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, -1));
                    Set Status(Event Player, Null, Unkillable, 99999);
                End;
                Create Effect(If-Then-Else((Event Player).is_downed, All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Winston Primal Rage Effect, Team 1, Eye Position(Event Player), True, Visible To Position and Radius);
                Create Effect(If-Then-Else((Event Player).is_downed, All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Ring, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).revive_timer, >=, 8), Color(Red), Color(Yellow)), Eye Position(Event Player), 5, Visible To Position and Radius);
                Create Progress Bar HUD Text(If-Then-Else((Event Player).is_downed, All Players(Team 2), Empty Array), If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).revive_timer, >=, 8), Multiply((Event Player).death_timer, 2.5), Multiply(Subtract(8, (Event Player).revive_timer), 12.5)), If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).revive_timer, >=, 8), Custom String("{0} {1} needs to be revived!", Hero Icon String(Hero Of(Event Player)), Event Player), Custom String("Reviving {0} {1}...", Hero Icon String(Hero Of(Event Player)), Event Player)), Right, -0.01, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).revive_timer, >=, 8), Color(Red), Color(Yellow)), If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).revive_timer, >=, 8), Color(Red), Color(Yellow)), Visible To Values and Color, Default Visibility);
                Create Icon(If-Then-Else((Event Player).is_downed, Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Not((Current Array Element).shop)), Empty Array), Eye Position(Event Player), Skull, Visible To and Position, Color(Yellow), True);
                Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, potions_max, 9, 200);
            End;
        End;
        If(And(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Torbj√∂rn)), Not((Event Player).enemy_ID)));
            Teleport(Event Player, Global.compressBakeMatcher);
        End;
        Abort If(Or(Or((Event Player).enemy_ID, Compare((Event Player).boss_ID, ==, 4.4)), And(Is Dummy Bot(Event Player), Compare(Team Of(Event Player), ==, Team 2))));
        Wait Until(Compare(Global.phase, >, 0.5), 99999);
        Create Effect(If-Then-Else(And(And(Or(Has Status(Event Player, Phased Out), Has Status(Event Player, Invincible)), Not(And(Compare(Hero Of(Event Player), ==, Hero(Reaper)), Is Using Ability 1(Event Player)))), Not(Is In Spawn Room(Event Player))), All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Baptiste Immortality Field Protected Effect, Team Of(Event Player), Event Player, True, Visible To Position and Radius);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, immune_effect, Last Created Entity);
    }
}

rule ("rein stand charge") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        Reinhardt;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).boss_ID == 4.4;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).bright, >=, 3), Random Real(1, 2), Random Real(3, 5)), Ignore Condition);
        Wait Until(Not(Has Status(Global.boss, Rooted)), 99999);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, target, Random Value In Array(Filtered Array(All Living Players(Team 2), Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element)))));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location, Ray Cast Hit Position(World Vector Of(Up, (Event Player).target, Rotation And Translation), Add(World Vector Of(Up, (Event Player).target, Rotation And Translation), Multiply(Direction From Angles(Random Real(0, 360), 0), 10)), Null, Event Player, True));
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, boss_target_location_2, Ray Cast Hit Position(World Vector Of(Up, (Event Player).target, Rotation And Translation), Add(World Vector Of(Up, (Event Player).target, Rotation And Translation), Multiply(Direction Towards((Event Player).boss_target_location, World Vector Of(Up, (Event Player).target, Rotation And Translation)), 100)), Null, Event Player, True));
        Create Beam Effect(All Players(All Teams), Echo Focusing Beam, (Event Player).boss_target_location, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2, Team 1, Visible To);
        Set Player Variable At Index(Event Player, boss_effects, False, Last Created Entity);
        Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards((Event Player).boss_target_location, (Event Player).boss_target_location_2), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Pickup Effect, Color(Red), Position Of(Event Player), 2);
        Stop Forcing Player Position(Event Player);
        Wait(0.05, Ignore Condition);
        Teleport(Event Player, Global._extendedGlobalCollection);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Wrecking Ball Piledriver Impact Sound, Color(Red), (Event Player).boss_target_location, 200);
        Wait(0.5, Ignore Condition);
        While(Not(Is Using Ability 1(Event Player)));
            Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ability 1));
            Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Wait(0.5, Ignore Condition);
        Teleport(Event Player, (Event Player).boss_target_location);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Pickup Effect, Color(Red), Event Player, 2);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Tracer Recall Reappear Sound, Color(Red), (Event Player).boss_target_location, 200);
        Destroy Effect(First Of((Event Player).boss_effects));
        Destroy Effect(Value In Array((Event Player).boss_effects, True));
        Wait Until(Not(Is Using Ability 1(Event Player)), 5);
        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Pickup Effect, Color(Red), Position Of(Event Player), 2);
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Start Forcing Player Position(Event Player, Add(World Vector Of(Vector(0.5, True, -2), Global.boss, Rotation And Translation), Multiply(Multiply(Up, Sine From Degrees(Global.pentagram_angle)), 0.5)), True);
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Bad Pickup Effect, Color(Red), Event Player, 2);
        Start Facing(Event Player, Facing Direction Of(Global.boss), 1000, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
        Loop If(Is Alive(Global.boss));
    }
}
