rule ("mercy bewitching grasp") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        Mercy;
    }
    conditions {
        Weapon(Event Player) == 1;
        Is Button Held(Event Player, (Event Player).button_damageboost) == True;
        (Event Player).has_status == False;
        Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 2) == True;
    }
    actions {
        If(Is Firing Primary(Event Player));
            Cancel Primary Action(Event Player);
        End;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, is_grasping, True);
        While(And(And(And(Is Button Held(Event Player, (Event Player).button_damageboost), Compare(Weapon(Event Player), ==, 1)), Not(Is Firing Primary(Event Player))), Not((Event Player).has_status)));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_target, First Of(Sorted Array(Filtered Array(All Living Players(Team 1), And(And(And(Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position(Current Array Element), All Barriers Block LOS), Compare(Angle Between Vectors(Facing Direction Of(Event Player), Direction Towards(Subtract(Eye Position(Event Player), Facing Direction Of(Event Player)), Current Array Element)), <, 30)), Not(Has Status(Current Array Element, Phased Out))), Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, Current Array Element), <, If-Then-Else(Is Using Ultimate(Event Player), 30, 15)))), Angle Between Vectors(Facing Direction Of(Event Player), Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position(Current Array Element))))));
            Damage((Event Player).damage_target, Event Player, 15);
            Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
            Damage((Event Player).damage_target, Event Player, 15);
            If(Or(Not(Is Button Held(Event Player, (Event Player).button_damageboost)), Compare(Weapon(Event Player), ==, 2)));
                Break;
            End;
            Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, is_grasping, False);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_target, Null);
    }
}

rule ("mercy bewitching grasp chain") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
        Has Status(Event Player, Phased Out) == False;
        Is Using Ultimate(Global.mercy) == True;
        (Global.mercy).damage_target != Null;
        Event Player != (Global.mercy).damage_target;
        Array Contains((Global.mercy).scrolls_equip, 2) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Create Beam Effect(If-Then-Else(And(And(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Global.mercy).damage_target), <=, 10), Is Alive((Global.mercy).damage_target)), Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Global.mercy).damage_target), All Barriers Block LOS)), All Players(All Teams), Empty Array), Moira Grasp Connected Beam, (Global.mercy).damage_target, Event Player, Team 2, Visible To Position and Radius);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, grasp_effect, Last Created Entity);
        While(And(And(Is Using Ultimate(Global.mercy), Is Alive(Event Player)), Compare((Global.mercy).damage_target, !=, Null)));
            If(And(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, (Global.mercy).damage_target), <=, 10), Is In Line of Sight(Eye Position(Event Player), Eye Position((Global.mercy).damage_target), All Barriers Block LOS)));
                Damage(Event Player, Global.mercy, 15);
            End;
            Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Destroy Effect((Event Player).grasp_effect);
    }
}

rule ("mercy flying broomstick") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
        Is Using Ability 1(Global.mercy) == True;
        (Event Player).broomsticked == False;
        Array Contains((Global.mercy).scrolls_equip, 3) == True;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare(Speed Of(Global.mercy), >, Multiply(10, Add(True, Multiply(Value In Array((Global.mercy).potions, 3), 0.05)))));
            If(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, Global.mercy), <, 5));
                Abort If(Has Status(Event Player, Phased Out));
                Damage(Event Player, Global.mercy, 40);
                Apply Impulse(Event Player, Add(Add(Normalize(Velocity Of(Global.mercy)), Direction Towards(Global.mercy, Event Player)), Vector(0, 1.2, 0)), 20, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
                Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Doomfist Rising Uppercut Impact Sound, Team 1, Event Player, 200);
                Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Doomfist Rising Uppercut Impact Effect, Team 1, Event Player, 1);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, broomsticked, True);
                Wait(2, Ignore Condition);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, broomsticked, False);
            End;
        End;
        Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

    actions {
        Create Dummy Bot(Hero(Zenyatta), Team 2, 10, Event Player, Up);
        Set Player Variable(Last Created Entity, zomnic, 2);
    }
}

rule ("roadhog recycling") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        Roadhog;
    }
    conditions {
        Is Crouching(Event Player) == True;
        Health(Event Player) > 100;
        Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 2) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, Multiply(Multiply((Event Player).damage_dealt, If-Then-Else((Event Player).nano, 1.5, 1)), 2));
        Wait Until(Or(Not(Is Crouching(Event Player)), Compare(Health(Event Player), <=, 100)), 99999);
        Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, Multiply((Event Player).damage_dealt, If-Then-Else((Event Player).nano, 1.5, 1)));
    }
}

rule ("roadhog recycling 2") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        Roadhog;
    }
    conditions {
        Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 2) == True;
        (Event Player).ammo_cache != Ammo(Event Player, False);
    }
    actions {
        If(And(And(Compare((Event Player).ammo_cache, >, Ammo(Event Player, False)), Is Crouching(Event Player)), Compare(Health(Event Player), >, 100)));
            Set Player Health(Event Player, Subtract(Health(Event Player), 100));
        End;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, ammo_cache, Ammo(Event Player, False));
    }
}

rule ("roadhog chain reaction 1") {

    }
}

rule ("roadhog roar") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        Roadhog;
    }
    conditions {
        Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 4) == True;
        Is Using Ability 2(Event Player) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Cancel Primary Action(Event Player);
        Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 2), 10);
        Heal(Event Player, Event Player, 300);
        If(Not(Global.roar));
            Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Winston Primal Rage Effect, Team 2, Event Player, True, Visible To Position and Radius);
            Modify Player Variable(Event Player, roar_effect, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
            Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Winston Primal Rage Sound, Team 1, Event Player, 200, Visible To Position and Radius);
            Modify Player Variable(Event Player, roar_effect, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
            Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Winston Primal Rage Sound, Team 1, Event Player, 200, Visible To Position and Radius);
            Modify Player Variable(Event Player, roar_effect, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
        End;
        Set Global Variable(roar, 5);
        Chase Global Variable At Rate(roar, False, True, None);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_received, 40);
        Set Damage Received(Event Player, Multiply((Event Player).damage_received, If-Then-Else((Event Player).nano, 1.5, 1)));
        Set Player Variable(All Players(Team 1), target, Event Player);
        Wait Until(Not(Global.roar), 99999);
        Stop Chasing Global Variable(roar);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, damage_received, 100);
        Set Damage Received(Event Player, Multiply((Event Player).damage_received, If-Then-Else((Event Player).nano, 1.5, 1)));
        While(Compare((Event Player).roar_effect, !=, Empty Array));
            Destroy Effect(First Of((Event Player).roar_effect));
            Modify Player Variable(Event Player, roar_effect, Remove From Array By Index, False);
        End;
    }
}

rule ("roadhog beware") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        Roadhog;
    }
    conditions {
        Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 5) == True;
        Is Using Ultimate(Event Player) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Knockback Dealt(Event Player, 0);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, speed, Add(200, Multiply(Value In Array((Event Player).potions, 3), 10)));
        Set Move Speed(Event Player, Multiply((Event Player).speed, Subtract(True, Multiply(0.5, Compare((Event Player).speed_boosted, >, False)))));
        Wait Until(Not(Is Using Ultimate(Event Player)), 6);
        Set Knockback Dealt(Event Player, 100);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, speed, Add(100, Multiply(Value In Array((Event Player).potions, 3), 5)));
        Set Move Speed(Event Player, Multiply((Event Player).speed, Subtract(True, Multiply(0.5, Compare((Event Player).speed_boosted, >, False)))));
    }
}

rule ("reaper marked for death") {
    event {
        Player Dealt Damage;
        Team 2;
        Reaper;
    }
    conditions {
        Event Ability == Button(Primary Fire);
        Array Contains((Event Player).scrolls_equip, 1) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable((Event Player).death_mark, damage_received, Subtract(130, Multiply(15, Global.difficulty)));
        Set Damage Received((Event Player).death_mark, Multiply(((Event Player).death_mark).damage_received, If-Then-Else(((Event Player).death_mark).nano, 1.5, 1)));
        Wait(False, Ignore Condition);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, death_mark, Victim);
        Set Player Variable(Victim, damage_received, Multiply(Subtract(130, Multiply(15, Global.difficulty)), 1.25));
        Set Damage Received(Victim, Multiply((Victim).damage_received, If-Then-Else((Victim).nano, 1.5, 1)));
    }
}

rule ("reaper the reapers scythe") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Is Meleeing(Global.reaper) == True;
        Array Contains((Global.reaper).scrolls_equip, 2) == True;
    }
    actions {
        While(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, Global.reaper), >, 5));
            Wait(Global.wait, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Abort If(Not(Is Meleeing(Global.reaper)));
        If(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, Global.reaper), <=, 5));
            Damage(Event Player, Global.reaper, If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, Global.reaper), <=, 2.5), 45, 75));
    }
}

rule ("reaper the reapers scythe visual") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        Reaper;
    }
    conditions {
        Is Meleeing(Event Player) == True;

        Set Player Variable(Event Player, scythe_length, Null);
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, scythe_angle, -10);
        Chase Player Variable Over Time(Event Player, scythe_angle, 130, 0.3, None);
        Chase Player Variable Over Time(Event Player, scythe_length, 5, 0.05, None);
        Wait(0.4, Ignore Condition);
        Chase Player Variable Over Time(Event Player, scythe_length, False, 0.1, None);
        Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
        Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, scythe_angle);
        Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, scythe_length);
    }
}

rule ("mystery skull") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase == 9;
        Global.sombra_egg == False;
        Is True For Any(All Players(Team 2), Compare(Distance Between(Current Array Element, Vector(-5.36, 2, -40.78)), <, 3.5)) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(sombra_egg, 1);
        If(Compare(Global.difficulty, ==, 3));
            Abort If(Compare(Global.dialogue_priority, >, True));
            Set Global Variable(dialogue_priority, 1);
            Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, True);
            Wait Until(Not(Global.main_dialogue), 99999);
            Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, False);
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Sombra), Custom String("..........................."), 1), Array(Hero(Sombra), Custom String("...You are worthy."), 1), Array(Hero(Sombra), Custom String("Witness me bequeath to thee this mystery key."), 1), Array(Hero(Sombra), Custom String("Ask no more ''Which door is it for?'', for I forgor."), 1.5)));
            Call Subroutine(main_dialogue);
            Set Global Variable(dialogue_priority, False);
            Set Global Variable(sombra_egg, 2);
            Small Message(All Players(Team 2), Custom String("Obtained mystery key!"));
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Sombra Translocator Disappear Sound, Team 1, Vector(-5.36, 4, -40.78), 200);
            Set Global Variable(map, Vector(54.45, 11.53, -100.12));
        Else;
            Abort If(Compare(Global.dialogue_priority, >, True));
            Set Global Variable(dialogue_priority, 1);
            Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, True);
            Wait Until(Not(Global.main_dialogue), 99999);
            Set Global Variable(is_dialoguing, False);
            Set Global Variable(active_dialogue_list, Array(Array(Hero(Sombra), Custom String("..........................."), 1), Array(Hero(Sombra), Custom String("...I only care for those who dare to bear the despair of a nightmare."), 1), Array(Hero(Sombra), Custom String("You are all not worthy."), 1.5)));
            Call Subroutine(main_dialogue);
            Set Global Variable(dialogue_priority, False);
            Set Global Variable(sombra_egg, 4);
    }
}

rule ("mystery door") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.sombra_egg == 2;
        Global.phase >= 9;
        Global.phase <= 12;
    }
    actions {
        Modify Global Variable(mystery_door, Add, 0.1);
        If(Compare(Global.mystery_door, >=, 15));
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Hanzo Sonic Arrow Initial Pulse Sound, Team 1, Global.map, 200);
            Set Global Variable(mystery_door, False);
        End;
        If(Is True For Any(All Players(Team 2), Compare(Distance Between(Current Array Element, Global.map), <, 2.3)));
            Set Global Variable(sombra_egg, 3);
            Small Message(All Players(Team 2), Custom String("A clicking sound was heard..."));
            Play Effect(All Players(All Teams), Brigitte Repair Pack Armor Sound, Team 2, Global.map, 200);
            Create Effect(All Players(All Teams), Ring, Color(White), Global.map, 2.4, Visible To Position and Radius);
            Set Global Variable At Index(skull_effect, True, Last Created Entity);
        End;
        Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("enter mystery door") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.sombra_egg == 3;
        Is True For All(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element))), Compare(Distance Between(Current Array Element, Global.map), <, 2.3)) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(sombra_egg, 4);
        Teleport(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 1), Compare((Current Array Element).enemy_ID, >, False)), Global.compressBakeMatcher);
        Teleport(All Players(Team 2), Vector(54.93, 11.21, -102.17));
        Create Dummy Bot(Hero(L√∫cio), Team 1, -1, Vector(54.44, 11.21, -122.39), Up);
        Set Player Variable(Last Created Entity, boss_ID, 5);
        Destroy Effect(Value In Array(Global.skull_effect, True));
        Big Message(All Players(All Teams), Custom String("The Brazillager"));
    }
}

rule ("brazillager throttle") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;
        L√∫cio;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, random, If-Then-Else(Is In Line of Sight(Vector(54.44, 11.21, -122.39), Eye Position(Event Player), Barriers Do Not Block LOS), Direction From Angles(Add(Horizontal Angle From Direction(Direction Towards(Position Of(Event Player), Vector(55, 11.21, -118))), Random Real(-90, 90)), 0), Direction Towards(Position Of(Event Player), Vector(55, 11.21, -118))));
        Wait(Random Real(0.2, 1), Ignore Condition);
        Loop;
    }
}

        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 1;

        Press Button(Event Player, Button(Ultimate));

        Restart Match;
    }

rule ("dialogue chan") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.phase > Null;
        And(Entity Exists(Global.dialogue_bot), Global.dialogue_bot) == False;
    }
    actions {
        Create Dummy Bot(Hero(Reinhardt), Team 1, False, Global._extendedGlobalCollection, Up);
        Set Global Variable(dialogue_bot, Last Created Entity);
    }
}

rule ("wait time") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.wait != Multiply(0.03, Number Of Living Players(Team 1));
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(wait, Multiply(0.03, Number Of Living Players(Team 1)));
    }
}

rule ("console check") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        Team 2;
        Mercy;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).button_rez == False;
        Magnitude Of(Throttle Of(Event Player)) > 0;
    }
    actions {
        If(Is True For All(Array(X Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player)), Z Component Of(Throttle Of(Event Player))), Not(Modulo(Current Array Element, 1))));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, button_damageboost, Button(Secondary Fire));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, button_rez, Button(Ability 2));
        Else;
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, button_damageboost, Button(Ability 2));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, button_rez, Button(Secondary Fire));
    }
}

rule ("restart no players") {
    event {
        Player Left Match;
        All;
        All;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        If(Compare(Filtered Array(All Players(Team 2), Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element))), ==, Empty Array));
            Restart Match;
    }
}
